might certaynly yt myght called vnhappy batayle man giueth lo uyng ye grekes euery man repor teth shame p eneas kyng yta lye iij yere eneas troy destroyed ye grekes came ytalye xx shyppes dyd myghty batayles man wedded priam doughter elinsuram made god errour comyn people man came iulius cezar octauianus augustus p vlixes eloquent man amonge grekes many perylles see went home penelopem moost faythful moost chaste woman redde grekes perisshed wretchedly destroyed troye bothe water londe wente homewarde agayn pryncypall date theyr wrytynge vyctory wrote theyr hystoryes wrytynges thus anno primo v secudo c post troiam captam thyrde yere abdon iudge israel p circa annum mundi iiij xxv et ante christi natiuitate c lxxiiij obeth chrystes lyne sone vnto boo rehersed mathewe p samson ye xv iudge regned xx yere sason ye strogest man yt euer delyuered israell philystyens meruaylous strength men trowed ben hercules et ei nurabilia oa vide iudic xiij p anno mundi iiij lxxv et ante christi natiuitatem c xiiij iesse sone obeth lyne chryst otherwyse called ysay fa der dauid tyme lyued notable man honeste kyng ne grete gouer nour many tymes made mencyon holy scripture hym descended chryst sauyour p tyme hely iudge bisshop israel whiche ij sone ophni phi nees corrected sufficiently punisshed bothe lorde slayne ye philisties hely fell sete brake necke hely iudge next samson lignage aron yt fyrst bysshop god electe ythamar lignage dured c xx yere yt whiche lignage hely fyrst bysshop abiathar last vide plura j regum tyme saul kynge israell mayster hystoryes iosephus viij boke saul ye fyrst kyng israel regned xx yere whiche kynge good man electe god afterwarde wretchedly fayled slayne thre sone hylles gylboy p ye tyme saul samuel iudge phete israel holy man borne barayn moder many daye mynystred afore lorde chylde age hygh bysshop iudged israel ye dayes lyfe ye pro phete god two kynges enoynted saul fyrst dauyd samuel alone moyses redde prayed theyr enemyes olde testamet samuel saul ben dyuers opynyons isoder sayth ye samuel saul ruled israel xl yere iosephus viij boke mayster storyes sayen samuel iudge xij yere alone hy saul regne xx yere vide plura j xe guin ascanius vij kyng ytaly sone eneas buylded ye cite albion called kyng albanon ascanius gate siluius viij kyng ytaly whiche siluius fader vnto brute kynge brytayn called englonde leue kynges ytalye dyd lytell noble thynges tyll co men romul remus ye buylded rome shall kynges come agayn cede ye cronycles englonde yt whiche namely boke made p venys padua buylded tyme ye resydue troyans p homere ye grete poete tyme yt whiche wrote fayned gloryously many lesynge p incipit regnum britannie nunc dicitur anglia p may ye se englonde fyrst began albyon albyon p afore wyll speke brute shall shewed londe englonde fyrst named byon cause named noble londe sirrie noble kynge myghty man grete renome yt called dioclesyan well worthely hy gouerned ruled noble chyualry yt conquered londes hym almoost ye kynges worlde hy attendaut befell thus yt dioclesian spoused getyll damoysel yt wonder fayre yt vncles doughter labana loued hym reason wolde yt gate xxxiij doughters yt whiche ye eldest called albyne damoyselles whan came vnto age came fayre yt wonder whereof dioclesian anone let make somnynge comaunded lettres kynges yt helde hym sholde come certayn daye lettres conteyned make feest royal whiche daye thyder came brought admyrats prince duke noble ch ualry feest royally arayed lyued ioye myrth ynough yt wonder wyte befell thus ye dyoclesyan thought mary doughters amonge kynges yt ye solempnite spake dyd albyne eldest doughter systers rychely maryed xxxiij kynges yt lordes grete honour solempnite whan done euery kynge toke wyfe ladde theyr owne coutre made quenes befell thus afterward yt dame albine became stoute sterne tolde lytel pryce lorde hyy scorne despyte wold wyll wold haue owne wyll dyuers mater systers euerychone bare euyll agaynst theyr lordes yt wonder wyte moche yt thought theyr husbondes hye parentage come theyr fader kynges yt theyr lordes wold haue chastysed fayre maner vpon al loue frendshyp yt shold amende theyr euyll condicyons nought dyd theyr owne wyll thynge yt lyked power wherfore xxxiij kynges vpon tyme often tymes bette theyr wyues wende wold haueamended theyr tatches wyckednes suche condicions fayre speche warnynge dyd ye worse betynges eftsones moche worse wherfore kyng yt wedded albyne wrote tatches condicyons wyfe albyne lettre sent dyoclesyan fader whan kynges herde albynes lorde sente lettre dioclesyan anone sente lettres sealed theyr seales condicyons tatches theyr wyues whan kynge dioclesyan sawe herde many complayntes doughters sore ashamed became wonderssy angry wroth toward doughters thought myght amende mysoyd anone sent lettres xxxiij kynges yt sholde come hym brynge wt theyr wyues euerychone certayn day wolde chastyse theyr wyckednes yf myght ony maner wyse ye kynges came ye tyme daye tho set bytwene hym kynges dioclesyan receyued wt moche honour made solem e feest vnto vndernethe lordshyp thyrde daye solempnite ye kynge dioclesyan sent xxxiij doughters yt shold come speke hym chambre wha come spake theyr wyckednes theyr cruelte angerly reproued blamed said yf wolde chastysed sholde lose loue euermore whan ye ladyes herde al became abasshed gretly ashamed sayd theyr fader yt wolde make amedes departed theyr faders chambre albyne ye eldest syster ladde chambre tho made voyde al yt therin yt psone amonge systers togyder thasayd albyne fayre systers well knowe yt kyng fader v hath reproued shamed despysed bycause make v obedyent husbondes certaynly yt shall neuer whyles ye ilyue syth come hyer kynges blode myn husbonde whan thus said systers sayd ye sayd albyne well wote fayre systers yt husbondes haue coplayned vnto fader vpon v wherfore hath v thus foule reproued despysed wherfore systers couseyle yt night whan husbodes ben bedde wt one assent kytte theyr throtes may pea better may vnder faders power tha ony el anone ye ladyes consented grauted counseyle whanyght comen lordes ladyes went bedde anone theyr lordes ept kytte theyr husbodes throtes shewe whan dioclesian theyr fader herde thynge became wroth ryght furyously agaynst doughters anone wole haue brent harons lordes rrye counseyled suche straytnes owne doughters shold boyde ye londe euermore neuer sholde come agayne dyd dioclesyan yt theyr fader anone comauded go shyppe delyuered itayles halfe yere whan done systers wente shyppe sayled forth ye see betoke theyr frendes appolyn yt theyr god longe sayled see yll last came arryued yle yt wyldernes whan dame yne come ye londe systers byne went fyrst forth ye shyppe sayd systers moche ye eldest syster copany first londe haue take moche name alb ne wyl londe called albion owne name anone systers grauted good wyll went ye shyppe ye systers toke londe albion theyr syster called went vp downe foude neyther man ne woman ne chylde wylde beestes dyuers kyndes whan theyr ttayles dispruded sayled fedde herbes fruytes season yt yere ued best myght yt toke flesshe dyuers beestes bera wonder fa e desyred mane company mane kynde fay ed wexed wonder couragyous kynde desyred mannes company ony solace myrth whan deuyll yt per yued went dyuers coutries toke body ye ayre lykyng nature sh men came ye londe albion lay woman shad tho nature vpon conceyued brought forth gyautes whiche one called gogmagog another langerigan named dyuers name maner came forth borne horryble gyautes albion dwelled caues hylles theyr wyll londe albion lyked vnto ye tyme brute arryued came totnes yt yle albion brute coquered discofyted ye gyautes aboue sayd p explicit prima par p begyneth brute goten slewe fyrst moder fader conquered albyon named brytayne owne name called englonde name engyst saxonye brute came brytayne aboute xviij yere hely knowen ye noble cite grete troy noble knyght man grete power called eneas whan ye cite troy lost destroyed grece eneas meyny fledde then came lombardy tho lorde gouernour londe kyng hyght latyne another kynge ye hyght turocelyne strongly warred vpon kynge latyne ye oftentymes dyd hym moche harme whan kynge latyne herde yt eneas come receyued hym moche honour hym helde moche herd hy wyst well yt noble knight worthy body dedes eneas helped kynge latyne wa shortly tell well worthely dyd slewe turocelyne dyscomfyted hym people whan done kyng latyne gaue ye londe turocelynes noble man eneas maryage lauyne doughter moost fayrest creature ony man wyst lyued togyder ioye myrth dayes theyr lyues p ascanius sone eneas wedded wyfe vpon gate sone called siluine siluyne whan coude reason man vnwytyng fader agaynst wyll acqueynted hym wt damoysel cosyn lauyne kynge latynes doughter ye quene eneas wyfe brought damoysell chylde whan ascanius fader wyst anone let enquyre wysest maysters gretest clerkes chylde damoysell sholde brynge forth answered sayd sholde brynge forth sone shold kyll bothe fader moder dyd moder dyed berynge hym whan chylde borne fader let call hym brute ye maysters sayd sholde moche harme sorowe many dyuerse place sholde come grete honour worshyp kyng ascanius dyed whan god wolde siluyne sone receyued londe made hym wonder ly well beloued among people wha brute siluynes sone xv yere olde went vpon daye fader playe solace brute shold haue shotte vnto hart arowe myshapped glanced brute slewe fader p brute dryuen londe helde hym grece whan mischauce befallen ye people londe made grete sorowe sore dyspleased bycause therof droue brute ye londe wolde suffre hym amonge whan sawe might abyde went then grece foude vij thousande men ye kynrede troye comen grete blode story telleth men woman child whiche holden thraldome bondage kyng pandras grece ye deth achylles betrayed slayne troy brute woders fayre man stronge huge age gladde chere semblaut also worthy body well beloued amoge people kyng pandras herde speke goodnes condicyons anone made hym dwell hym brute became wonder preuy moche beloued ye kynge dwelled longe tyme kynge ye last troy brute spake togyder kynrede lygnage acqueyntauce complayned vnto brute theyr sorowe theyr bondage many shame ye kynge pandras done brute sayd vpon tyme ye lord lignage stronge man myghty ye capytayne gouernour wyll become men fulfyll al comau dementes brynge v wret chednes bondage wyll fyght wt kyng trouth grace ye grete god shall ouercome hym shall make kynge londe homage shall holde euermore brute tho grete pyte theyr bondage yt brought pryuely went fro ye kynges courte tho troy went put woodes moutaynes helde sente vnto kynge pandras sholde gyue lycence departe safely lode kyngdom wolde longer dwell bondage whan kyng pandras herde sore vexed anoyed tho sware wolde e euerychone ordeyned grete power went towardes fyght brute men manly defended fyersly fought slewe kynges men none escaped toke ye kynge put hym pryson ordeyned couseyle amonge selfe myght wt kynge sayd sholde put deth sayd sholde exyled londe sayd yt sholde brent spake wyse knyght yt called mempris sayd brute troy yf kyng pandras wolde yelde hym haue lyfe couseyle yt gyue vnto brute duke souerayn doughter ge og wyfe maryage hondred shyppes well arayed treasour golde syluer corne wyne moche nede one thynge go londe ordeyne v lode el none kynrede yt come v shall neuer haue pea londe amonge grece haue ayne many theyr knyghtes frendes euermore warre dyscord shall amonge v brute tho folke consented gladly ye couseyle thyge tolde kyng pandras haue lyfe grauted moche demaunded anone gaue vnto brute fayre lady gennogen doughter wyfe hondred shyppes moche vytayles afore ordeyned tha brute toke wyfe men forsoke londe grete went see wynde weder theyr wyll came thyrde daye yle called logres brute anone sent men londe espye ye maner ye coutrce founde olde cite wasted forlet neyther man woma therin dwellynge myddle cyte foude olde temple fayre lady called diane goddesse came agayne vnto brute tolde hym seen foude couseyled hym go sacrifyce vnto dame diane wont gyue answere thynge asked namely vnto honour sacryfyce brute wente vnto yt ymage sayd diane noble goddesse thynge hast thy myght wyndes water woodes feldes thynges ye worlde maner beestes ben therin vnto make prayer ye couseyle tell place shall haue couenyent place dwell folke shall make honour fayre temple noble wherin ye shall alwaye honoured whan done prayer diane answered maner brute sayd go euen forth thy way ouet see frauce towarde west ye shal fynde yle called albion yle becompassed see man may come therin shyppes londe wont dwell gyauntes wyldernes londe destenyed ordeyned people p coryn became brute man kynge goffar discomfyted whan brute answere diane goddesse anone let wyde vp ancres sayled hye see wha men sayled xx dayes foude fall besyde coost see men kynrede troy theyr souerayne mayster called coryn whan brute wyst whens toke wt moche ioye shyppes ladde forth hym coryn became brute man hy dyd homage loge sayled forth see tyll came gascoyne anone arryued ye hauen lyegers dwelled viij dayes rest amende theyr sayles nede ty dynges soone came kyng goffar lord londe moche people straunge londe arryued londe hauen lyegers wherfore sore angred anoyed came arriued londe without lycence leue anone ordeyned hym grete power dryue brute destroye hym people ye kynge goffar dyscomfyted people hymselfe fledde fraunce haue helpe socour yt tyme regned fraunce xij kynges xj assembled grete power belpe goffar fyght agaynst brute goffar dwelled wt kynges frauce halfe yere meane tyme goffar frauce brute company destroyed londe gascoyne let take treasour kynge goffar made men neuer theles whan ye two hoostes mette togyder brute folke helpe hym selfe turyn cosyn coryn well manly defended within whyle slayne frenshmen moo two anone tho alyue fledde away batayle turin brute cosyn slayne brute let bury hym worthely whan space ye castell yt made tho let call yt castell tour bycause name turin yt buryed yet vnto daye noble cite yt called tour whan kyng goffar wyst yt turyn deed came agayne wt men gaue stronge batayle brute brute men wery fightyge yt might longer endure went castel wt men made gate fast saue toke couseyle amoge sholde brute coryn gaue couseyle ordeyned pryuely coryn shold go busshe hym wode tyll morowe yt mornynge whan brute sholde fyght wt enemyes coryn shold come wt folke ye one syde slee ye harme yt myght morowe dawnynge daye brute wente castel fought fyersly wt enemyes manly defended within lytell tyme brute men slewe viij hondred kynge goffer men came corin wt busshemet company smote groude wolde stande abyde ye kynge goffar company hondred xv whiche nobly buryed castell tour buryed turyn cosyn p brute arryued totnes yle called albyon wrastlyng bytwene coryn gogmagog wha done brute wold longer dwell fyght lose men kyng goffer people myght euery day encrease moo moo brute men lessed therfore toke men wente vnto see wynde weder theyr wyll fyfth daye arryued hauen cornes came realme yt called albyon founde neyther man woman saue grete gyauntes dwelled mountaynes cauernes brute sawe londe fayre ly kynge good also hym people diane ye goddesse behyght hym therof brute wonder gladde let assemble vpon daye folke make solempne sacrifyce grete feest ye honour reuerece diane goddesse whiche couseyled hy fyrst come londe wha done theyr sole pnite sate theyr meet vpon daye came vpon xxx gyauntes slewe xxx brute men brute anone stert vp fought gyauntes slewe euerychone saue one yt called gogmagog mayster gyautes stroger hyer ony brute kepte hym wrastle corin man greter hyer ny brute men gyrdelstede vpwarde gogmagog corin vndertoke wrastle togyder went wrastled loge tyme last gogmagog helde coryn fast yt brake two rybbes syde wherfore coryn sore angry toke gogmagog bytwene armes cast hym downe vpon roche soo gogmagog aboute dyuerse place yt myght fynde good place couenable myght buylde make cyte hym folke last came fayre ryuer whiche called temmes brute began buylde fayre cyte called newe troye remembraunce grete enemyes gyue batayle lotryn sente cambar broder yt sholde come vnto hym ye power myght make helpe hym auenge broders deth dyd good wyll whan came togider toke theyr waye pryuely go seke kynge humbar myght fynde hym befell kynge humbar besyde water grete ryuer folke dysporte hym came lotryn cambar broder theyr folke sodeynly ony theyr enemyes wyst whan humbar sawe come sore adrad moche men wyst afore also vnarmed anone humbar drede water drowned hymselfe dyed men flayne moche escaped one awaye lyue therfore water called humbar euermore shall longe worlde standeth bycause kynge humbar drowned therin locryn went shyppes toke golde syluer moche founde vnto himselfe pylfre gaue vnto folke hoost founde one shyppes fayre damoyfell whiche kynge humbars doughter called estrylde whan kynge lotryn sawe toke hym bycause grete beaute fayrnes sawe ouertaken loue wolde haue wedded tydynges came corin anone thought auenge hym lotryn moche lotryn promised hym wedde guentolyn doughter corin haste toke waye newe troy vnto hym sayd thus lotryn certes ye rewarde full euyll ye paynes haue fader brute wher fore syth wyll auenge yt drewe swerde wolde haue slayne lotryn ye kyng damoysel went bytwene made accorded maner lotryn sholde take guentolyn corins doughter wyfe lotryn dyd neuertheles maryed wente pryuely estrylde gate doughter called abram befell yt anone corin dyed whan deed lotryn forsoke guentolyn wyfe made e quene guentolyn dep fro grete wrath cori e seased londe owne ha or moche faders heyre toke homage men londe afterwarde assembled grete hoost myghty men auenged vpon lottyn lorde yt cassibalon grauted slayne romayne deth kymbalyn regned gynder sone good man worthy hygh herte wolde paye rome trybute kynge cassybalon graunted vnto iulius cesar wherfore emperour claudius cesar sore anoyed greued ordeyned grete power romayns came londe conquere trybute myght strengthe haue kynge kynge gynder armager broder assembled gadered grete hoost togyder britos gaue batayle ye emperour claudius slewe romayns grete plente emperour afterward one called hamon sawe theyr people fast slayne pryuely cast awaye owne armes toke armes deed bryton armed hym therwith came batayle ye kynge thus sayd syr good herte goddes loue romayns enemyes anone shall slayne discofyted kyng gaue kepe wordes bycause ye armes vpon hym wend ben bryton traytour euer helde hym nexte kynge pryuely vnder ye sholder arme smote kynge wherfore kynge dyed fell downe erth wha armager sawe broder deed cast awaye armes toke hym broders armes came batayle amonge ye brytons badde hertely fyght fast lay downe romayns ye armes wende ben kyng gynder afore slayne yt wyst began brytons fyersly fyght slewe romayns ye last ye emperour soke felde fledde fast myght wt folke wynchestre fals traytour hamon yt slayne kyng fast anone began flee ye haste might armager ye kynges broder pursued hym full fyersly fyers herte droue hym vnto water toke hym anone smote bothe handes foot heed hewed body peces let cast hym called gosselyn scaped went then rome seke socour helpe destroye sarasyns destroyed londe romayns sayd yt ben often anoyed theyr sendyng folke britayne helpe briton wold bysshop gosselyn went then without ony socour helpe went ye kyng lytell brytayne yt called aldroie ye thyrde kyng gowan meriedok sayd bysshop prayed kynge aldroie helpe socour ye kynge pite herte whan herde ye bysshop fledde chrysten men slayne grete brytayne ye paynyms sarasyns grauted hym costantyne bro er helpe hym power folke cha dyd araye hors harneys shyppes thynge yt neded vyage whan thynge redy called ye bysshop sayd hym take costantyne broder vpon couenaut yt yf god gyue hym grace discofyte ye infydeles ye shall make hym kyng ye bisshop grauted wt good wyll costantyne bysshop toke leue ye kyng aldroie betoke hym god toke xij inen went theyr shippes sayled towarde grete britayn arryued totnes whan ye briton herdethese tydynges socour came glad ordeyned huge people went receyued wt moche honour p gowan anone wyst ty dynges assembled farasyns came agaynst gaue batayle costantyn slewe hym wt owne handes sarasyns dyscomfyted slayne yt none escaped excepte couerted god p constantyne kynges broder lytel britayn crowned kynge grete brytayne worthynes anone ye batayle went london crowned constantyne kyng londe ye bysshop gosselin set crowne heed oynted hy belongeth kyng tha began christedom londe agayn anone wha kyng constantyn crowned spoused wyfe rouseyle ye brytons begate herthre sone fyrst called costance ye seconde aurilambros thyrde vter constance yt elder broder wha came hym monke wynchestre constatyne theyr fader slayne treason befell vpon tyme pehyte came hym vpon daye message sayd wolde speke kynge pryuely cou seyle kyng let oyde chambre men within abode moo kynge pehite made countenauce though wolde haue spoken kyng eere shewe hym longe knyfe went meruaylously chambre chambre last man wyst b roman whan kynges men wyst theyr lord deed made moche sorowe yt wyst moche two sone aurilambros vter yonge none myght kynge thyrde broder monke chestre sayd nger erle westler thought pryuely herte subry e kynge hymselfe wente wynchestre constance monke sayd hym costance qued fader deed two brethern ben wt gosselyn bysshop london nourysshe yonge neue may kyng wherfore cou seyle ye forsake habyte come shall make suche meane vnto brytons ye shall made kynge londe p constance moche tyll forsoke ab ot went hym anone crowned kyng ye assent brytons kynge constance whan crowned made kynge wyll ne knewe lytell ye worlde coude thynge knyghthode axed made vortyger chefe mayster couseyler gaue hym power ordeyn moche ye realme aperteyned yt hymselfe thynge entermedled onely bare name kyng wha vortiger sawe ye lode warde gouernauce owne wyll thought preuy treason slee costance ye kyng myght hyselfe crowned made kyng regne let sende hondred knyghtes pehytes ye worthyest ye londe helde wt hym dwell kepers body wolde go londe ordeyne thynges yt appertayned kyng vortiger honoured moche ye hondred knyghtes moche gaue golde syluer ryche iewelles robe horse thyges plente wherfore helde hym lord dyd kyng vortiger told yf myght kyng ye treason wold make rychest ye londe ye last grete gyftes gyuen largely cryed ye court yt vortiger better worthy kyng tha costance wherfore vortiger made semblaut ben wroth departed then ye courte sayd must go elles thinges traytour sayd came kynge vortiger sholde go chambre take nyghtes rest ronewen engistes doughter came cup golde hade kneled kynge sayd hym wassayll kynge wyst mene e shold answere therto moche hym selfe none brytons coude speke none englysshe vnderstande spake language briton yet neuerthelesse latiner tolde kynge full vnderstandynge wa sayll shold answere drynke hayll fyrst tyme wassayll drynke hayll came vp londe fro tyme vnto tyme well vsed realme englonde whan kynge vortiger behelde grete beaute fayre lady ronewen kneled hym toke vp layde bothe armes aboute necke thryes swetely kyssed anone ryght damoysell moche confusyon hym selfe therfore ye brytons became wrothe bycause spoused woman mysbyleue wherfore went fro hy wold thynge yt p vortimer vortigers sone made kyng engyst dryuen vortimer poysoned engist went kent seased ye londe hades hym men became within lytel whyle grete power moche people men wyst litel tyme whiche ye kyges men whiche engystes wherfore brytons hym drede sayd amonge yf ne toke couseyle bytwene londe shold destroyed engist people vortiger ye kyng begote fyrst wyfe thre sone ye fyrst called vortimer seconde catagren ye thyrde passent brytos one assent chose vortimer theyr lorde souerayne crowned hym kyng wold suffre vortiger longer regne bycause alyauce bytwene engist hym brytons ordeyned grete hoost dryue engist company ye londe gaue hym thre batayles fyrst kent lorde seconde tetford ye thyrde shyre side colchestre moor batayle mette catagren horne engystes broder eche slewe moche ye coutre gyuen longe horne vortiger wha spoused cosyn made fayre castell called horne castell owne name vortimer sore anoyed broders deth anone let cast downe ye castell ye erth stynted nyght daye tyll dryuen engyst people londe ronewen doughter made grete sorowe craftely spake nexte kyng vortimer pryuely entreated many gyftes gaue kynge empoysoned dyed london fourth yere regne lyeth p briton chose tyme vortiger theyr kynge engist came londe agayne fought togyder vortimers dethe brytons theyr comyn assent made vortiger agayne theyr kynge vpon couenaunt sholde neuer suffre engist none come agayne londe whan done ronewen quene pryuely sent lettre engist empoysoned vortimer vortiger lorde bare agayne crowne regned sholde come agayne londe wel arayed moche people auenge hym vpon brytons wynne londe agayne myght strength whan engist herde tydynges made grete ioye apparayled hym hastely xv thousande men boughty euery batayle came londe whan vortiger herde tell engist comen agayn grete power londe assembled brytons went mete engist gyue hym batayle engist dredyng ye brytons sore dyscofyted hy prayed vortiger loue day sayd comen londe fyght haue londe agayn yf myght accord wt brytos kyng vortiger couseyle brytons grauted hym loue day ordeyned brytons yt loue daye shold holden besyde salysbury hyll engyst sholde come thyder iiij c knyghtes moo ye kyng wt many ye wysest men londe yt daye ye kyng came wt couseyle ordeined engist warned knightes pryuely eche sholde put longe knyfe hose whan sayd fayre syrs tyme speke loue pea euery man anone shold drawe knyfe slee bryton slewe lxj knyghtes moche sorowe many escaped ye kynge vortiger nede p mason haste fette began ye werke vpon ye hyll breigh certes thus befel ye werke yt mason made daye fe l downe ye night wyst myght therof ye kynge sore anoyed yt chauce wyst wherfore let send ye wysest clerkes lerned men wale yt myght foude shold hym tell wherfore ye foudamet fayled vnder werke shold hym tell best wha wyse men longe tyme studyed sayd ye kyng yt sholde seke childe borne woman yt neuer man chylde sholde slee tempre blode morter werke sholde werke euer endure without ende p ye kyng let seke merlin wale speke hym whan kyng herde co mauded messenger anone go wale seke chylde yf myght fynde hym sholde brynge hym forth vnto hym recorde wytnes thynge taken lettres ne destroubled man ne lette ye messenger went then spedde fast came town called karmardyne passed forth theyr waye foude two chyldren xxiiij yere age chydynge togyder hasty wordes one sayd donebat quod ye wronge stryue ye haue wytte ne reason haue certes merlyn quod wytte ne reason make forte men tell comynly yt ye haue thyge god almyghty syth ye neuer fader euery man knoweth well moder p messenger kynge vortiger whan herde stryfe bytwene ye two gromes asked yt stode besyde whens merlyn borne also nourysshed hym tolde yt grete gentylwoman karmardyne called adhan moder none knewe fader whan kynges messenger herd tydyges went anone hym wardeyne ye towne tolde hym ye kynges wyll shewed hym lettre wherfore comen thyder merlyn moder anone fetched wardeyn ye towne comauded sholde go ye kynge messenger merlyn moder went then came vnto ye kyng receyued wt moche honour ye kyng asked lady yf yt chylde sone hym begate lady answered full tenderly wepynge sayd neuer company man worldly syr sayd whan yonge mayden faders chambre wt grete lignage copany ofte tymes went sporte left alone chambre wolde go forth brenynge ye sonne came tyme fayre bacheler entred chambre alone came wyst neuer ne yet knowe ye dores fast barred wt dyd game loue myght power defende hy ofte came ye fore sayd maner yt begate chylde neuer myght wyte p answere merlyn vpon kynges castell wolde stande whan merlyn herde moder sayd spake kynge maner p syr begoten aske ye falleth none knowe tell ye cause wherfore brought wherfore ye haue sent certes quod kynge wyse couseylers haue done vnderstande ye morter werke haue begon behoueth tepred blode foudament shall fayle euermore syr said merlin wyll ye slee blode tempre morter ye quod kynge elles shall neuer castell stade couseylers tell answered merlyn kyng syr said let come wyse couseylers wyll preue saye well ne truly whan wyse men comen merlyn asked yf blode cause make ye werke stande endure wyse men abasshed coude answere sayd merlyn ye kyng syr shall tell cause wherfore werke thus falleth may stande vnder moutayn ye buylde toure grete pond water bottom ye ponde vnder water two dragon one whyte reed fyght togyder agaynst werke ye depe myne tyll men come pond men take away ye water ye shal se dragon haue tolde yt fight togyder agaynst werke cause wherfore foudament falleth kyng anone let dygge vnder tyll ye men came ponde let away ye water foude two dragon merlin tolde egerly f ught togyder whyte dragon egerly assayled reed layde hym strongly sythen comynge agayne sarons recouered londe helde euermore droue brytos dyd lode al theyr wyll destroyed chrystendom londe ye fyrst ioye wt theyr comyng turned grete domage sorowe two bretherne aduentures vj last kynges regne englonde londe sholde ende sir sayd merlyn yere incarnacyon iesu chryst cc xv shall come lambe wynthestre shall haue whyte tongue true lyppes shall haue wryten hert holynes lambe shall make many goddes house shall haue pea ye moost parte lyfe shall make one ye fayrest place ye worlde tyme shall fully made ende ende lyfe wolfe strauge londe shall hy moche harme sorowe warre ye labe shall mayster helpe reed foxe shall come north west shall ouercome hym wolfe shall dye water tyme lambe shal lyue whyle shal dye seed shal strauge londe londe shall without gouernour lytell tyme tyme shall come dragon medled mercy also woodnes shall haue berde gote shall gyue englonde shadowe shall kep lond colde hete one fote shall set wyke london shall embrace habytacyons shall open mouth towarde wale tremblynge hydour mouth eeres shall stretche towarde many haby acyons countrees breth shall full swete strauge londe tyme shall ryuers renne blode brayne shall make place londe walles shall moche harme vnto seed tyme shall come people northwest durynge regne shall ladde wycked hare dragon shall crowne kyng afterwarde shall flee ouer see without comynge agayne drede ye dragon tyme sonne shall reed blode men shall se worlde shall betoken grete pestylence deth folke dynt swerde people shall faderles tyll tyme ye dragon dye hare shal ue warre agaynst hym vnto ende lyf shall fully ended tyme dragon shall beholde tyme best body worlde shall dye besyde march strauge londe londe shall dwell faderles without good gouernour men shall wepe deth yle shepey vnto hauen mar yl wherfore ala shall theyr songe faderlesse folke shall ouer lyue londe destroyed dragon shall come gote kar shall haue horne berde syluer shal come nosethrilles domp shall betoken hungre sorowe grete dethe people moche londe begynnynge regne shall wasted gote shall go ouer frauce shall open floure lyfe deth tyme shal aryse egle cornewayle shall haue fethers golde pryde shall wt pere londe shall despyse lordes blode shal flee shamefully bere gauerscch shal made brydges men vpon costes see stone shall fall castelles many townes shall made playne tyme shall seme yt bere shall brenne batayle shall done vpon armes see felde ordeined shelde batayle shal dye many whyte hedes wherfore batayle shall called whyte batayle foresayd bere shall gote moche harme shall come south west blode shal gote lese moche londe tyll tyme shendshyp shall ouercome hy shall clothe hym lyon skyn shall wynne lost therto people shall come northwest shall make gote sore aferde yt shall grete plexite shall auenge hy enemyes counseyle two owles fyrst shall peryll vndone olde owle shall go away certayn tyme shall come agayn lode two owles shall grete harme many one shal couseyle gote arere warre agaynst foresayd bere last gote owles shall come burton vpo trent shall go ouer drede bere shall flee swan wt hym fro copany burton towarde north shall wt harde shoure tha shall swanne taken slayne sorowe bere taken heded nexte vnto nest shall stande vpon broken brydge sonne shall cast bemes many shall hym seke vertue shal come hym shall dye sorowe care people londe many londes shall vpon hym bolder afterward two owles shall moche harme soresayd floure lyfe shall lede dystresse shall passe ouer see frauce make pea bytwene gote flourdelyce shall dwell tyll tyme seed shall come seche shall styll tyll tyme shall clothe grace shall seche owles put despytous dethe shall gote brought dysease anguysshe sorowe shall lyue lyfe gote shall come wyndsore bore shall haue heed whyte lion hert piteous lokynge vysage shall rest seke men brest shal stauchyg thurst thursty word shal gospel herynge shall meke lambe first yere regne shal haue grete payne iustyfye vntrue tyme shall lode multyplyed wt aliautes bore thrugh fyersnes hert shall make wolues become lambes shal called worlde bore holynes fyersnes noblenes mekenes shall mesurably shall vnto bourgh ierusalem shall whette tethe vpon gate parys vpon foure londes spayn shall tremble drede gascoyn shall swete frauce shall put wynge grete tayle shall rest englonde softly almayne shal quake drede bore shal gyue mantel two townes englode shal make ryuer ren wt blode brayne shal make many medowes reed shall gete moche auncesters dyd dye shall bere thre crownes shal put lond grete subieccyon shal recouered tyme bore deed dough tyne shal buryed coleyn londe shall replete good bore shal come lambe hauyng foot leed heed brasse hert loppe swynes skyn hard tyme londe shall pea ye fyrst yere regne shal make cite yt ye worlde shal speke lambe shall lese wolfe grete part londe shall recouer gyue lordshyp egle lond egle shal well gouerne tyll pryde shall ouercome hym ala sorowe shall dye broders swerde shall ye londe fall foresayd lambe yt shall rule ye lode pea lyfe shal dye londe shall fulfylled wt goodes labe shall come mold warpe cursed god mouth caytyf coward hare shal haue elderly skyn gote vengeaunce shall fall vpon hym synne fyrst yere regne shal haue al good grete plente londe shall haue grete praysyng lond tyll tyme shall suffre people lyue ito moche pryde wtout chastysynge wherfore god wyll wroth tha shall aryse vp dragon north shal full fyers shal meue warre agaynst moldwarpe gyuynge hym batayle stone dragon shal gadre copany wolfe comynge west meue warre agaynst moldwarp syege shal dragon bynde theyr tayles gyder shall come lyon londe yt shal fall copany shall tremble ye londe yt shall called englode aspen lefe tyme shall castels kest vpon tamyse shal seme seuerne shal drye deed bodyes shall fall therin iiij chefe flodes englonde shall ren blode grete drede shall anguysshe yt shal aryse ye moldwarp shall flee ye dragon lyon ye wolfe shall dryue away londe shall wtout moldwarp shall haue maner power saue onely shyppe wherto may go yt shall gyue ye thyrde parte londe haue fourth parte rest pea shall lyue sorowe lyfe tyme tyme ye hote bath shal become colde yt shall moldwarp dye auenturously sodemly ala sorowe shall drowned flode see seed shall become faderles strange londes euermore shall lond departed thre partes yt say wolfe ye dragon ye lyon shal euer shall londe called londe coquest shal ye tyght heyres englonde ende p tyme merlin tolde kyng arthur kynges guillomer irlonde ordeyned grete power irysshmen arryued scotlonde fast kyng arthur lay wt hoost p kyng see arryued fast king arthur wt hoost anone wyst therof went towardes hym gaue hy batayle ouercame hym guillomer fled wt men agayn irlonde wha done arthur returned agayn place lefte scottes wold haue slayne bysshops abbot folke coutre ladyes open heded come kyng arthur cryed hy mercy sayenge gentyl kyng ye mayntayner christe dom haue pite v euen chryste deth ye gete worship slee chryste folke therfore haue mercy v haue moche sorowe saxon haue passed countree ynough haue taken castels slayne beestes eten moch harme haue done v yf ye slee v cryenge mercy sholde grete dyshonour ye haue done ynough v haue ouercome v goddes loue suffre v lyue haue mercy chryste people byleue chryst ye whan kyng arthur herd sorowe pite gaue lyf lymme wtout ony harme fell foot tha ked hym became lyege men toke homage kyng arthur turned agayn wt host came yorke abode duryng vyage gaue al logres aloth yt spoused syster plente gyftes tha gawen cosyn yoge age al men serued hym warre gaue ryche gyftes thankynge theyr good seruyce p kyng arthur spoused gueneuer erles cosyn cornewayle conquered irlonde whan kynge arthur brought londe pea rest good state well euery coutree tha toke wedded wyfe called gueneuer made quene fayre lady gentyl cador erle cornewayle nourysshed chambre yt cosyn neuer childre togyder neuertheles king arthur loued full well anone wynter past let assemble grete host baron gouernauce romayns taken londe noble knyght worthy body called froll whan wyst kyng arthur came ordeyned hoost grete power fought kynge folke dyscomfyted fledde vnto parys entred cite closed gate helde hym wha arthur wyst froll gone parys pursued came thyder besyeged hym cite stronge well arayed therin defended well manly kynge arthur dwelled moneth moche people cite dispended theyr vytayles wtin grete hunger became amonge dyed wonder thycke within cite hunger came vnto froll prayed hym accorded wt kyng arthur haue pea wolde yelde vnto hym cite also froll saw might longer holde cite agaynst theyr wyll trusted gretly vpon owne strength sent kynge arthur sholde come fyght wt hym body body sholde departe frauce bytwene two kyng arthur anone grauted none people vndertoke batayle hym orow bothe came well arayed wtout parys shold fyght anone togyder smote fyersly well fought bothe sydes man coude deme better befell froll gaue arthur suche stroke kneled groude wheder wold froll rome yt owe ye worlde deme hast neuer yet tyme proued ne assayed strength ye romayns therfore thou shall lytell tyme iulius cesar conquered ye londe brytayn toke therof truage folke haue longe thy almoost xj yere man taught armes made many bokes elles lytell hym wryten p gregorius v pope man almoost thre yere gregory made pope instaunce emperour otto thyrde cosin whan ben lytell whyle pope chirche many batayles spered bycause deuoute almyghty god sayntes gaue myghty worshyppyng vnto relykes sayntes oftentymes visyted holy place man crowned gregory cosyn last decessed rome p anno domini iiij nota siluester second pope gregory iiij yere made pope helpe deuyll whome dyd homage sholde gyue hym thynge desyred called gylbert enemy gate hym grace ye kynge frauce made hym bysshop remensis anone deposed gate grace emperour made bysshop rauennie pope ende anone haue put theyr hope fals deuyls yet men trust saluacyon certayne demonstracions sepulture ye grete penauce yt dyd last ende made iohannes xix pope hym fyue yere two dyd lytel thyges p henricus ye fyrst emperour almayn xx yere henry duke barry accordyng chosen blyssed fame good name whiche redde many duke barry holy men onely absteynynge flesshly desyres also vertuous lyuyng henry syster holy whome gaue wyfe vnto kynge hungary brought hungary vnto right byleue chrysten fayth wyues name san ro ogundis whome lyued virgyn dayes lyfe made many batayle well ytaly almayn agayust rebelled prospered ryght wysly euermore last blyssed ende decessed lyf saynt laurence wyfe put ensamples bycause theyr holy vertuous lyuynge p benedict pope iohn xi yere man grete stryfe dayes put put benedictus deed seen holy bysshop wretched fygure grete payne fygure sayd trusted thynge mercy god thynge profyted hym done hym goten extorcyon vniustly tha bysshop lefte bysshopryche drede sight went monastery lyued vertuously dayes p iohanes ye xx pope hym xi yere lytell profyted p kyng knoght dane deth eldred knoght daue bega regne edmund irensyde yt king eldredes sone fyrst wyfe ordeyned grete power men began warre kynge knoght dyd many tymes ofte warre stroge harde ye wonder wyte quene emme yt dwelled westmynster grete drede two sone alured edward lest sholde destroyed ye warre wherfore sente ouer see normandy duke richard theyr vncle dwelled safete pea loge tyme p edmund irensyde knoght dane warred fyersly togyder ye last accorded maner sholde departe realme bytwene dyd loued togyder lyke two bretherne p kyng edmund irensyde slayne treason traytour yt called edryth stratton regned kyng edmud irensyde knoght ye dane thus befel afterward yt ye yere accorded moche loued togyder wherfore fals traytour enuy loue bytwene whose name edrith stra grete lorde yt edmunde irensydes man hym helde londe neuerthelesse thought betraye lorde make knoght kyng londe entent rychely auauced hym well beloued wherfore prayed lorde edmunde irensyde daye hym ete kyng hym curteysly grauted hym came prayer meet kyng ryally serued dyuerse mete drynkes whan nyght came sholde go bedde kyng toke owne meyny went chambre shold take nyghtes rest loked aboute hym sawe fayre ymage well made semblaut archer bowe bent hande ye bowe fyne arowe kynge edmund went nere beholde better whan anone ye arowe smote hym body slewe kynge ye engyn made slee owne lorde traytoursly whan kynge edmund thus deed slayne regned x yere people made moche sorowe body bare glastenbury buryed hym fals traytour edrith anone went ye quene kynge edmundes wyfe wyst lordes deth toke two sone fayre yonge lorde goten one called edwarde edwyne ladde wt hym london toke kyng knoght yt sholde wyl told hy subtylly slayne king edmund bycause ye knoght sholde haue londe englonde p thou fals traytoure hast yu slayne true broder true bycause man moost loued worlde heed shall thy trauayle well rewarde thou hast deserued anone let hym taken boude hym handes foot maner traytour let cast hym ryuer tamyse maner fals traytour ended lyfe kyng toke ye two chyldren put vnto abbot west mynster warde kepe tyll wyst best p kynge knoght sent bothe kyng edmondes sone denmarke slayne saued befel soone afterward kynge knoght londe handes spoused ye quene emme consent al baron fayre woman whiche eldredes wyfe duke syster normandy lyued togyder moche loue reason wolde kyng asked vpon daye couseyle quene best wt edmond irensydes sone syr sayd ryght heyres londe yf lyue wyll moche sorowe wt warre therfore let sende strauge londe aferre man may destroye king anone let call dane called walgar comauded hym sholde lede two chyldren denmarke ordeyne sholde neuer syr sayd walgar commaudement gladly shall done anone toke two chyldren ledde denmarke moche sawe chyldren wonder fayre ke grete pite ruth wold slee ledde ye kynge hungary nourysshe walgar well beknowen kynge well beloued anone kynge asked fro whens child walgar tolde hym sayd yt ye ryght heyres englonde therfore men wolde destroye therfore syr vnto comen seke mercy helpe soth yf may lyue men shall become shall holde theyr londe kynge hungary receyued moche honour let worthely kepte thus befell afterwarde edwyne ye yonger broder dyed edwarde elder broder lyued fayre man stronge large body gentyll curteys condicyons yt men loued hym edwarde ye cronycles called amonge englysshmen edwarde outlawe whan made knyght kynges doughter hungary loued moche goodnes fayrnes called hym derlynge kynge fader perceyued well loue bytwene two none heyr onely doughter kynge vouchedsafe doughter man well dyd hym loued well agayn gaue vnto hym good wyll edwarde spoused moche honour kyng hungary sent baron made solemp e feest ryche weddynge made men vnderstande yt edwarde sholde kyng decesse londe hungary whiche tydynges ryght glad edwarde begate vpon lady sone whiche called edgar helyng afterwarde doughter called margarete afterwarde quene scotlonde kyng scotlond called mancolin doughter called maud quene afterwarde englonde kyng henry fyrst sone conquerour wedded begate doughter called maud afterward empresse almayne maud came kyng englonde vnto daye called henry empresse sone yet edwarde doughter wyfe yt called christian nonne p kynge knoght yt proude man conquered way became afterwarde meke mylde haue ye herde edmunde irensydes sone yt king knoght wende ben slayne co mauded walgar kyng knoght handes realme englond denmark went vnto norway coquere londe kynge londe yt called elaf came people wende haue well kepte defended londe faught wt hym tyll last slayne yt batayle tha knoght toke londe hades wha coquered norway take feaute homage came agayne englonde helde hyselfe grete lorde yt hym thought worlde pere became proude hauteyne grete wonder p befell vpon daye herd masse west mynster wolde haue gone palays wawes tamyse swyftely came agaynst hym almoost touched foot sayd kyng proude herte comaunde water turne agayn elles shall make wawes comaudemet wold spare flowed heyght kyng proude herte wold flee water abode styll water bette wt yerde hande comauded ye water yt sholde go ferder co maudement water wold cese encreased kyng wete stode depe water whan sawe water wold comaudement wtdrewe hym stode vpon stone holdyng vp handes hye sayd herynge people god yt maketh see thus aryse hye kyng kynges mygh te moost caytyf deedly man may neuer dye thynge doth comaudement hym obeyeth yt god praye yt warraut knowlege caytyf feble power therfore wyll go vnto rome without ony longe lettyng wycked ne punysshe amende god clay londe holde none anone made redy heyre hyselfe went rome without ony lettynge waye dyd many almes dedes rome also wha ben done penauce synnes came agayn englonde became good man holy leuyng maner pryde lyued holy lyfe made two abbey saynt benet one englonde another norway cause loued saynt benet specyally ony sayt loued moche also saynt edmund kyng often gaue grete gyftes hous made ryche whan regned xx yere dyed lyeth wynchestre p anno dni xviij benedict ix pope iohannes grete lethour therfore dampned appered certayne man vnder meruaylous fygure horryble heed tayle lyke asse part body lyke beer sayd appered aferde man ye beestly lyuynge wha pope appere lyke beest p mane tyme grete diuisyon sclaudre chirche put two tymes ptholomeus noteth yt pryde bysshops euer euyl ende euer occasyon moche vnrest batayle p coradus fyrst emperour hery xx yere made many lawes comau ded pea kept moost straytly ony man erle ludolf accused fledde fro londe desyred lyue lyke chorle lyke gentylman yet meruaylously sone made emperour comaundement god agaynst wyl conradus last accorded toke conradus doughter wyfe p kynge harold leuer go fote ryde horsbacke knoght whome haue spoke two sone wyfe emme yt one called hardiknoght yt harold lyght fote yt men called hym comynly harold hare fote harold thynge manerd knoght fader set cheualry curteysy ne worship onely owne wyll became wicked yt exiled moder emme went flau dres dwelled wt erle wherfore broder hated echeother deedly whan regned ij yere hedyed lyeth west mynster p kynge hardiknoght haroldes broder harold hare fote regned broder hardyknoght noble knight worthy moche loued cheualry maner goodnes whan hardiknoght regned lytell whyle let vncouer broder harold smote heed made cast gonge body ta myse came fysshers toke bedy theyr nettes nyght bare hym saynt clemetes chirche buryed hym thus auenged hym hardiknoght broder thus kyng har diknoght large gyuer meet drynke table set euery daye thre tymes full ryall mete drynkes meyny came courte kyng hardiknoght sent emme moder made come agayn broder harold hare fote dryuen lond couseyle erle godwyn gretest lorde englonde nexte kynge moost rule bycause spoused doughter kyng knoght begoten fyrst wyfe whan quene dryuen englond came erle flaundres called baldewyne cosyn foude thyge neded vnto tyme went agayne englonde kynge hardiknoght sent sone made come agayne moche honour kyng hardiknoght whan regned v yere dyed lyeth west mynster p vylany dane dyd englysshmen wherfore fro tyme dane made kynge londe deth kyng hardiknoght moche ne chylde body begoten le baron asseinbled made couseyl neuer man yt dane though neuer grete man amonge shold neuer kyng englonde despyte yt done englysshmen euer yf englyshmen da ne happened mete vpo brydge englyshmen shold hardy mene fote stande styll tyll dane passed forth ouer yf englyshmen bowed theyr heedes reuerence vnto dane sholde haue ben beten defouled suche despytes vylany dyd dane englysshme wherfore driuen londe hardiknoghtes deth lorde myght mayntayne maner auoyded dane englonde neuer came agayn erles baron theyr comyn assent counseyle sente vnto normady seke two bretherne alured edwarde dwellynge wt duke rycharde theyr vncle entent crowne alured elder broder make hym kyng englonde thynge make ende erles baron made theyr othe erle godwyn westsex falsly traytoursly thought slee two bretherne anone shold come englond entent make harold sone kynge whiche sone begoten wyfe kyng hardiknogh te doughter dane godwyn went pryuely southhamton mete two bretherne theyr landynge thus befell yt messenger yt went normandy foude onely alured eldest broder edwarde broder gone hungary speke cosyn edwarde outlawe edmund irensydes sone messenger said aluted erles ba ron englond sent hy shold boldly come englode receyue realme king hardiknoght deed dane dryuen londe p godwyn fals traytour toke alured vpon gildesdown whan came normandye kynge englonde caused hym martyred yle ely whan alured herd tydyges thaked god toke shyppyng haste myght passed see arryued south hamton godwyn fals traytour whan traytour sawe comen welcomed hym receyued hym moche ioye sayd yt wold lede hym london baron englonde hym abode make hym theyr kynge went theyr waye towarde london whan came gyldesdowne tho sayd traytour godwyn vnto alured take hepe aboute bothe lefte syde ryght syde ye shal kyng suche hondred mod forsothe sayd alured behyght yf kyng shall ordeyne make suche lawes wherof god man shall well apayed tray tour comauded men wt hym whan comen vpon gyldesdown shold slee aluredes company came hym normady take alured lede hym yle ely put bothe eyen heed afterward brynge hym deth dyd slewe company nombre xij gentylmen comen alured fro normandy toke alured yle ely put eyen rent wombe toke chefe bowel put stake groude ende bowel fastened therto nedyls yren pricked good thylde made hym go aboute stake tyll yt bowel drawen body dyed alured treason erle godwyne whan lordes englond herde wyst alured sholde haue ben theyr king put deth fals traytour godwyne wonder wroth swore bytwene god holy name sholde dye worse deth tha dyd edryth whiche sholde occupy place bothe two stroue amonge selfe henry emperour came rome deposed made clement second pope whome made anone crowne hym sayd romayns sholde neuer wtout assent chose pope v beynge pope syxth put many men saye grego ry holy man p damasus second clement xxiij dayes man vsurper popery che dyed sodeynly anone romayns asked haue pope almayns sholde haue none harde herted myght enclyne entent emperout whiche sayd sholde pope chosen yf wolde counseyle eleccyon put holy man leo conscyence refused anone chosen comyn assent leo put chryst forme lasar owne bedde morowe founde thynge p saynt edwarde confessour aluredes broder kynge englonde wha done baron englond sent another tyme normandy edward sholde come englond moche onout edwarde chyldhode loued hey god hym dradde honeste clennes ladde lyfe hated synne deth whan crow ned anoynted wt ryall power forgate good maners condicyons fyrst vsed forgate good customes maner honour ne rychesse ne maner hygnes euer gaue hym goodnes well loued god holy chirche passyng maner thynge poore men also loued helde ben owne bretherne ofte gaue grete almes wt full good wyll p fyrst specyall loue god shewed saynt edward lyuynge befell daye went fro chirche westmynster herde masse saynt iohn ye euangelyst moche loued sayt iohn euangelist specyally god lady dyd ony saynt came hym pylgrym prayed hym ye loue god lady saynt iohn euangelyst good gyue hym kyng pryuely toke rynge fynger yt man perceyued gaue pilgrym receyued went then king edward made ye good lawes englonde yet ben moost vsed holden mercyable full pyte man myght p erle godwyn came agayne englonde agayne londe afterwarde saynt edwarde wedded doughter whan erle godwyn dwellynge denmark moche herde goodnes kynge edwarde full mercy pyte thought yt wolde go agayne englond seke haue grace good kyng edward mercy full myght haue agayn londe pea arayed hym moche myght put hym towarde see came englonde london ye kynge tyme lordes englonde helde parlyamet godwyn sent yt frendes ye moost gretest lordes lode prayed beseche ye kynges grace hym wolde graunte pea lode lordes lad hy ye kyng seke grace anone ye kyng sawe hym appeled hym treason deth alured broder wordes hym sayd traytour godwyn appele thou hast betrayed slayne broder alured certes syr sayd godwyn saue grace pea lordshyp neuer betrayed hym e yet lewe hy therfore put reward caurte fayre lordes sayd ye kynge ye lyeges erles baron londe yt ben assembled full well ye herde myn appele answere also godwyn therfore wyll ye awarde ryght erles baron gadred togyder awarde themselfe spake dy uersly among sayd neuer alyauce homage serment seruyce lordshyp bytwene godwyn alured whiche thynge myght hym drawe last deuysed demed shold put hym ye kynges mercy togyder tha sna ke erle leuerike couentre good man god worlde told reason maner sayd erle godwyn ye best frended man englonde ye kyng well myght gaynsayd without cou se yle godwyn alured neuer put deth wherfore awarde touchynge parte hymself sone euery v xii erles ben frendes go kynge charged moche golde syluer may bere bytwene handes prayenge kynge forgyue euyll wyll erle godwyn receyue homage yelde agayn londe accorded vnto awarde came euery golde syluer moche myght bere bytwene theyr handes kynge sayd forme maner theyr accorde theyr awarde kyng wolde gaynsaye moche ordeyned grauted cofermed erle godwyn accorded kynge agayne londes afterward bare hym well wysely kynge loued hym wonder moche hym full preuy within lytell tyme loued moche ye kynge spoused godwyns doughter made quene neuertheles though kyng wyfe yet lyued euer chastite clennes body wtout ony flesshely dede doynge wyfe ye quene also halfe ladde holy lyfe two yere dyed afterwarde kynge lyued lyfe without ony wyfe kyng gaue erledome oxford harolde godwyns sone made hym erle well beloued bothe ye fader preuy kynge yt myght ryght thynge wolde agaynst ryght wold thynge maner man good true conscyence therfore lorde iesu chryst specyall loue shewed hym p kynge edwarde sawe wyne kynge denmarke drowned see tyme leuacyon sacrament stode herde masse befell vpon whytsondaye kynge edwarde herde masse grete chirche westmynster leuacion iesu christes body men gadred chirche came nigh awter se ye sacrynge kyng lyft vp handes hygh toke vp grete laughter wherfore yt stode aboute hym began gretly wonder masse asked kyges laughter fayre lordes said kynge edward sawe swyne ye yonger kyng denmarke come see wt power haue comen englond warre vpon v sawe hym folke drowned see sawe leuacyon chrystes body bytwene preestes hades therof grete wye myght laughter withholde erle leuerich stode besyde hym leuacion openly sawe forme breed turne ye lykenes yonge childe toke vp ryght hande blyssed kynge afterwarde ye erle erle anone turned hym toward ye kynge make hym se holy syght sayd kynge syr erle well ye se thanked god haue honoured god sauyour vysybly iesu chryst forme man whose na blyssed worldes amen p rynge saynt edwarde gyuen poore pylgrym ye loue god saynt iohn euangelyst came agayne kynge edwarde noble man saynt edwarde regned xiii yere thus fell vpon tyme dyed ye two men englond gone ye holy londe done theyr pilgrymage goynge agayne theyr owne coutree came fro went waye mette pilgrym curteysly salewed asked londe coutree borne sayd englonde asked kyng englonde answered sayd good king edward fayre frendes sayd pylgrym whan ye come coutree agayne praye ye wyll go vnto kyng edwarde greet hym oftentymes name oftenty me thanke grete curteysy yt hath done namely ye ryng yt gaue whan herde masse westmynster saynt iohns loue ye euagelyst toke ye rynge toke pylgryms sayd praye go bere ryng take vnto kyng edward tell hym sende hym full ryche gyfte wyll gyue hym vpo xij daye shal come euermore dwell blysse wtouten ende syr sayd ye pilgryms man ye coutree dwellynge fayre frendes sayd iohn euangelyst dwellynge almyghty god kynge edward frende loue hym specyall bycause hath euermore lyued clennes clene mayd praye message fulfyll haue sayd whan sayt iohn ye euagelyst thus charged sodeynly voyded bothe theyr sightes thanked ye pylgryms almyghty god went forth theyr waye whan gone two thre myle bega ware wery set rest fell slepe whan well slepte one awoke lyft vp heed loked aboute sayd felowe aryse vp go waye sayd felowe certes sayd ye semeth yt ye coutre layde v owne rest slepe ierusalem thre myles toke vp theyr handes blyssed went forth theyr waye went sawe shepes herdes goyng wt theyr shepe spake none laguage englisshe good frendes sayd one ye pylgryms coutre lord therof anone shepeherdes answered sayd coutree kent englond whiche good kynge edward lorde pilgryms thanked almyghty god saynt iohn ye euangelyst went forth theyr waye came caunterbury then london foude kynge tolde hym ye begynnynge endynge moche saynt iohn charged thyges spedde ye waye toke ye rynge kyng edward receyued thanked almyghty god saynt iohn ye euan gelyst made hym redy euery daye daye daye departe lyfe whan god wold send hym p saynt edwarde dyed xij daye befel thus chryst masse euen holy man edward goddes seruyce matyns ye hygh feest became full seke morowe endured wt moche payne ye masse masse let hym ladde chambre rest hym hall amonge baron knyghtes myght come comforte solace wont worthy feest wherfore theyr myrth coforte amonge hall turned care sorowe bycause drad lese theyr good lorde ye kyng vpon saynt iohns daye ye euangelyst came nexte kynge receyued ryghtes holy chirche befalleth euery chrysten man abode mercy wyll god ye two pylgryms let come hym gaue ryche gyftes betoke god also ye abbot westmynster let come hym toke hym ryng honour god saynt mary saynt iohn euangelyst abbot toke put amonge relykes westmynster euer shall laye ye kynge seke tyll xij euen dyed good kyng edward westmynster lyeth whose loue god hath shewed many fayre myracle ye yere ye incarnacyon lorde chryst iesu lxv translated put shryne ye noble martyr saynt thomas caunterbury ictor seconde pope leo lytell hy wryten p henry seconde emperour first henry xvij yere man cosyn conrade borne wode twyes taken slayne wha childe god defended hy euermore whan made emperour made monastery ye place wode borne man vicyous man entred ytaly toke pandulphus ye prynce campany p ste phan ix pope victor ix monethes p benedictus hy toke dignite ye pope stephen strengthe kepte ix monethes decessed p henry thyrde emperour henry second henry vnquyete man many tymes troubled holy man gregory vij fyrst asked forgyuenes assoyled perseuered brought pope agaynst hym sayd heretyke gregory cursed hym chosers emperour chose duke saxon emperour whome henry batayle ouercame came rome pope pursued pope gregory cardynals also anone robert ye kynge naples droue hym then delyuered pope cardynals neuerthelesse yet man grete almes xij tymes fought batayle ye last dyed wretchedly put downe owne sone dyd men done p nycolas seconde pope benedicte two yere nycolas called couseyle agaynst archedeken turonosens whiche heretyke taught agaynst fayth erred sa crament couerted holy man coude neuer couerte discyples p nota p alexander seconde pope hy xij yere alexander holy man ordeyned vnder payne cursynge man shold preestes masse whome knewe man vt p xxxij dist preter hoc strife wt one codulo expulsed hy vsurper put hym symoner p harolde godwyns sone made kynge escaped fro duke normandy whan ayt edward gone worlde passed god worthely buryed apperteyned suche grete lorde baron londe wolde haue edward helingus sone edward outlawe edmud irensydes sone kyngr bycause moost called isap meridoc began make warre agaynst kynge edward cause syr payne tiptot ye wrongfully greued diseased ye foresayd bisap meridoc whan kynge edward herde sente lettres bisap meridoc sholde make warre sholde pea loue whan came agayne englonde wolde vndertake ye quarell amende mysdone foresayd risap meridoc despysed kynges co maundement spared sorowe myght ye kynges men englond anone taken ladde yorke drawen hanged felony p redressyng king edward made iustices clerkes done theyr falsnes droue ye iewes englonde theyr vsury mysbyieue whan kynge edward dwelled thre yere gascoyn desyre came hy go englonde agayn whan comen agayn many coplayntes made hym iustices clerkes done many wronges falsnes wonder whiche falsnes syr thomas weylonde kynges iustyce forswore englonde ye toure londo falsnes men put vpon hym wherof atteynt proued fals anone whan kynge done wyll iustices let enquyre espye iewes deceyued begyled people theyr synne falsnes vsury let ordeyn preuy parliament amonge lordes ordeyned amoge ye iewes shold voyde eng lode theyr misbyleue also theyr false vsury dyd vnto chrysten men spede make ende thynge comynalte englonde gaue vnto kynge xv peny al theyr goodes mouable iewes dryuen englonde went ye iewes frauce dwelled leue kyng philyp kynge frauce p kynge edwarde seased ye londe scotlonde cosent graute ye lordes scotlonde longe ye alexander kyng scotlonde scotlonde chefe lord whan kyng seased foresayd lordes scotlonde ye foresayd bayloll brus hastynges came kynges courte asked ye kynge whiche sholde kyng scotlonde kyng edward full gentyll true let chose vnto theyr kyng willyam waleys rybaud harlot comen vp nought englysshmen dyd moche harme p kyng edward thought myght best delyuer people taken gascoyne haste went hym ouer see flaundres warre handes towarde heuen kynge heuen gyue v mercy ye erthly kyng hath v forsaken frere prechour went hym castell tyll came place ended lyfe vnto shroue hy lyfe gentyll erle helde frere wonder fast clothes sayd hym fayre fader abyde v tyll deed flesshe quaketh drede deth sothe saye gentyl erle set hym vpon knee turned hym towarde ye eest rybaud called higone moston set hande vpon gentyl erle sayd despyte hym syr traytour turne toward ye scottes thy foule dethe receyue turned hym toward north noble erle thomas answered mylde voyce sayd fayre lordes shall wyll ye worde frere went hym sore wepynge anone rybaud wente hym smote heed xi kal apryll yere grace ccc xxi ala yt euer suche gentyll blode sholde put deth wtout cause reason traytoursly kynge counseyled whan fals couseyle ye spenser suffred syr thomas vncles sone put suche deth heded agaynst reason grete pite also yt suche noble kynge sholde deceyued mysgouerned couseyle ye fals spenser whiche maynteyned loselry honour also fyte disheryted also bycause yt spenser coueyted haue theyr lode wolde desyre wronge agaynst reason made ye kyng robert baldok fals pylled clerke chau celer englonde couseyle ye foresayd spenser fals yere lord ccc xxij scottes went hyd wodes mountaynes taryed ye englysshmen fro day day yt kyng myght maner thyge fynde playn wherfore many englisshmen ye vytayles dyed honger woders fast sod ynly goynge comynge namely ben thomas lacastre robbed men vpon lode whan kyng edward sawe yt vytayles fayled hym wonder sore dyscoforted bycause also yt men dyed might spede enemyes ye last came aga bycause taken good erle thomas lancastre ordeyned kynges comau demet englonde brynge power myght helpe hy agaynst scottes abbey beyghlonde whan fals traytour gadred people myght sholde haue come king abbey beighlond fals traytour ladde countree copelonde erledom lancastre went coutree robbed slewe folke myght ferthermore fals traytour taken grete gold syluer syr iames douglas agaynst kyng englond helpyng holdyng wt scottes whose treason kyng englond discomfyted beighlonde came thyder wherfore kynge toward hym wonder wroth let pryuely enquyre coutre aboute men enquyred espyed last trouth foude sought atteynt taken fals traitour good erle thomas lacastre hym tolde put dethe takynge burbrydge hym sayd yere done shold taken holden traytour holy man sayd wherfore kyng sent priuely syr anthony lucy knight coutree cardoyll sholde take syr andrewe herkela put hym deth bryng thynge ende kynge sente comyssyon andrewe taken cardoyll ledde barre maner erle worthely arayed swerde gyrde aboute hym boted sporred tha spake syr anthony maner syr andrewe sayd kynge putteth vpon moche hast benorped thy dedes dyd moche honour made erle cardoyll thou traytour thy lorde laddest people countree sholde haue holpe hym batayle beighlond thou laddest away coutree copelonde erledom lancastre wherfore lorde kynge discofyted scottes thy treason falsnes yf thou haddest comen betymes batayle treason dydest grete somme gold syluer thou receyued iames douglas scotte kynges enemy lorde kyng wyll ordre knyghthode whiche receyued thyne honour worship vpon thy body brought nought thyne estate vndone knightes lower degree may ware whiche lord hath hugely auaunced dyuers coutrees englonde may take ensample theyr lorde afterward truly serue commauded knaue anoue hewe sporres heles lette breke swerde ouer heed whiche kyng gaue hym kepe defende londe therwith whan made hym erle cardoyl let hy vnclothed furred tabard hode furred cote gyrdell wha done syr anthony sayd hym andrew sayd arte thou knyght knaue thy treason kynge wyll shalte hanged drawen thy heed smytten thy bowelles taken thy body brent thy body quartred thy heed sente londo shall stande vpon london brydge foure quarter shal sente mynde agayn vertue holy martyr p also god hath gyuen exepyls theyr goynge croked theyr handes theyr foot blynde also theyr fyght many seke folke theyr helth byuers dyseases loue martyr p also ryche certayne place englond redresse amende estate realme kyng edward answered sayd lordes sayd ye se full well lo haue seale gyue power ordeyne parlyament ye wyll toke theyr leue hym came agayn baron englonde whan kynges patent thynge shewed lordes ordeyned parliament shold westmynster vtas saynt hylary grete lordes englonde let ordeyne agaynst tyme parlyament sholde whiche daye parlyament kyng wolde come maner thynge set hymselfe assygned neuerthelesse baron sent vnto hym one tyme swore goddes soule wolde come one fote wherfore ordeyned grete lordes englonde sholde longer kyng depo sed sayd wolde crowne edward sone elder yt duke guyenne sent tydynges vnto kyng warde vnder syr iohn erle garen syr iohn bothun yt bysshop ely syr henry percy baron syr willyam trussell knyght erle thomas deposed ye withstande thanked god also bycause ye wold come parliament ye ordeyned westmynster owne lettre patent conteyned treate wt lyege men kyng sholde therfore comyns assent lordes englonde tell shold haue horne syluer berde whyte snowe droppe shold come nosethrylles yt sholde betoken moche harme honger dethe people grece losse londe begynnynge regne sholde hauted moche lechery sayd sothe ala honger among poore people stronge dethe amonge ty dyed strange londe sorowe warre scotlond afterward lost scotlonde gascoyn moche le chery dayes hauced p also merlyn sayd yt gote sholde seke floure tolde egle sholde come cornewayle sholde haue fethers golde pryde sholde haue pere shold despyse lordes blode shold dye bere gauersyche prophecy full well knowen foude soche egle vnderstande syr pyers ganaston erle cornewayle whiche wonder proude man despised baron englonde afterward heded gauersyche ye erle lancastre erle warwyk p merlyn tolde tyme sholde seme bere sholde brenne batayle shold vpon arme see felde arayed lyke shelde sholde dye many whyte hedes sayd sothe brennynge ye bere betokened grete drede cuttynge swerdes batayle myton came ye scottes maner shelde wynge slewe men religyon preestes seculers wher fore scottes called batayle despyte englysshmen whyte batayle p merlin sayd foresayd bere sholde gote moche harme yt sholde vpon ye south west also vpon blode sayd also yt gote shold lese moche dele londe tyll tyme shame sholde hym ouercome shold clothe hym lyon skynne sholde wynne agayne lost people sholde come north west yt sholde make hym fered hym auenge vpon enemyes counseyle two owles fyrst shold peryl vndone two owles sholde go ouer see strauge londe dwell certayn tyme shold returne agayn englond shold moche harme many one sholde couseyle ye gote meue warre agaynst foresaid bere gote owles sholde come arme ye see burton vpon trent sholde go ouer drede bere sholde flee swan copany bury towarde ye north vnkynde outpulter ye swan tha shold slayne wt sorow bere shold slayne full nye owne nest yt shold stande vpon poutfret vpon whome sonne sholde shede bemes many folke shold seke hym vertue sayd sothe ye good erle thomas lacastre borne north west cosyn ye kynge vncles sone lawe made ye kynge lese moche lode yt purchased wyl fully tyll ye last kynge toke therof shame hymselfe fylled wt cruelte gate agayne yt lost moche helpe folk comyng ye northwest drad auenged hy baron cou seyle ye two spesers yt afore lawed theyr wickednes came agayne frauce moche spenser couseyled ye kynge yt shold warre vpon thomas lancastre yt kyng spenser erle arundell theyr power mette thomas lancastre burton vpon trent hym discomfyted syr vmfrey erle herford company fledde foresayd thomas vmfrey theyr company burbrygge metynge syr andrewe herkela called ye vnkynde outpulter also syr symond warde erle yorke came met wt thomas latastre wt huge company discosyted disco siture crle herford slayne vpon brydge cowardly spere foudement erle thomas taken ladde poutfret
