also ye tresour yt syr edward carnaruan left many place englod wale wasted borne awaye without ye wyll kyng edward sone destruccion hym folke p also whose couseyle kyng gaue vp ye kyngdom scotlonde ye whiche realme kynges auncesters full sore trauayled dyd many noble theyr ryght delyuered dauid robert ye brus sone al ye right ryght ye realme al worlde wyst p also whome ye charter remembrauces yt right scotlode taken tresoury taken scottes kynges enemyes dysherytyng hym successours grete harme lyeges grete reprefe englysshmen euermore p also wherfore ame ione ye toure kyng edwardes syster disparaged maryed dauid yt robert ye brus sone yt traytour enemy englod whose couseyle taken enemyes handes englode p meane whyle good erle henry lancastre copany toke couseyle poyntes aboue said might amended ye worship ye king profyte ye profyte also lyeges p quene isabell coniectynge subtylte also mortymer let ordeyn parlyament salysbury parlyamet mortimer made erle marche agaynst baron wyll englonde preiudyce ye kyng crowne syr iohn eltham ye kynges broder gyrt swerde cornewayle tho called erle cornewayl euermore quene isabell cured moche anenst sone king yt ye warde ye foresaid syr edward londes parlyamet ye erle lancastre wold come ordeyned power agaynst quene isabell mortymer men london ordeyned v c men armes whan quene isabell wyst doynge swore god name full angerly euyll tyme thought vpon poyntes sent quene isabell mort mer theyr retynue ye kynges retynue ordeyned amoge huge hoost couseyled kyng vpon nyght rode xxiij myle towarde bedford ye erle lancastre company thought haue destroyed hym nyght rode besyde kyng sone knight armed drede deth done kynge vnderstande ye erle henry lacastre company wolde haue destroyed kyng couseyle euermore wherfore ye kyng somdele towardes hym heuy anoyed p whan ye erle marshall erle kent kynges broder herde tydynges ode message bytwene kyng graunted hym pea erle henry lancastre certayne raunsom x poude neuer payed warde ye lordes ye helde syr henry lancastre syr henry beamont syr fouk fitz war syr thomas rocelyn syr willyam trussell syrr thomas wyther aboute ondred knyghtes moo hym cosen ted ex led cou seyle quene isabell mor mer mortymer wayted haue theyr lode yf yt might ony maner coniecting co u moche wyll grete py e p kynge edwarde went ouer see homage kynge fraunce duchy guyen longe ye kyng frauce couseyle douzepers sent vnto kynge edward englonde sholde come parys homage reason wolde duchy guyen cou seyle lordes englonde kynge edward went ouer see ascencyon tyde came parys thyrd yere regne homage vnto kyng frauce kyng receyued homage made hym moche ioye worship wha kyng edward done homage hastely sente englonde quene isabell moder anone hastely came agayn englond vpon whytsonday wtout takynge leue kyng frauce wherfore wonder wroth p syr roger mortimer bare hym proudly wonder hye shall ye syr roger mortimer wygmore desyred coueyted hye estate kyng grauted hym called erle marche throughout lordshyp became proude hauteyn wold lese forsake name elder euer cause let call hym erle marche none comyns englonde durst call hy name called kynges crye men sholde call hym erle marche mortimer bare hy hauteyne proude wonder wyte also dysguysed hym wonder ryche clothes maner reason bothe shapynge werynge wherof englysshmen grete wonder maner myght contryue fynde suche maner pride sayd amoge comynly pryde sholde longe endure tyme sir geffrey mortimer mortimer sone let call hym kyng foly befell afterwarde dede full pryde wretchednes held roude table wale men came thyder couterfeyted doynge maner kyng arthur table openly fayled noble kyng arthur moost noble lorde renome world tyme yet came neuer none suche al noble knyghtes chrystendom dedes armes assayed dwellyng wt kyng arthur helde hym theyr lord souerayn well seen conquered batayle romayn called froll gate hym realme frauce slewe hym wt handes also faught gyaunt called dinabus slewe hym rauysshed fayre eleyn kynge howelles nece kynge lytell brytayn slewe batayle emperour rome called lucie assembled agaynst kynge arthur fyght hym moche people romayns phethis sarasyns man coude nombre discomfited story telleth p tyme comyn voyce spronge englonde coniectynge ordynauce frere prechers syr edward car naruan kyng edwardes fader whome gest telleth sayd alyue castell corf wherfore al comyns englode almoost sorowe drede whether wyst traytoursly mortimer done hym murdred p edmond wodstok erle kent kynges broder edward carnaruan heded wynchestre certayne tyme befell syr edmond wodstock erle kent spake vnto pope iohn xxij auinyon sayd almyghty god often tymes done thomas lone laneastre many grete myracles many men woman dyuerse maladyes vndone vnto worlde prayer brought theyr helth syr edmond prayed pope hertely wolde graut hy grace foresayd thomas might translated pope sayd nay shold translated vnto tyme better certyfyed clergy englonde seen theyr obedyence thynge god done loue saynt thomas lancastre suggestyon foresayd erle kent made hym whan edmond saw might spede purpose touchyng translacyon prayed hy couseyle touchyng syr edward carnaruan broder sayd longe ago king englonde thynge myght best done touching deliuerauce syth comyn fame englonde alyue safe whan pope herde hym tell syr edward alyue comauded erle vpon benyson sholde helpe wt power myght delyuered prison saue body myght brynge thynge ende assoyled hym copany pe na et culpa al tho holpe deliueraunce toke edmond wodstok leue pope came agayne englonde whan syr edmond comen frere prechers came sayd syr edwarde broder yet alyue castell corf vnder keping syr thomas gurney tho sped hym foresayd edmod fast might tyll came castel corf aqueynted hym spake fayre iohn daueryll constable castell gaue ryche gyftes haue acqueyntaunce hym knowe couseyle thus befel foresayd syr edmond prayed specially tell hym pryuely lorde broder syr edward yf lyued deed yf alyue prayed hy one haue syght hym syr iohn daueryll hye herted man full courage answered shortly syr edmond sayd syr edward broder helth vnder kepyng durst shewe hym man syth defended hy kynges half edward edwardes sone carnaruan also comaudemet quene isabell kynges moder syr roger mortymer shold shewe body man world saue onely vpo lyf lyme disheryting heyres euermore fals traytour falsly lyed warde take then lad castell berkeley syr thomas gurney comaudement mortimer tyll deed sayd syr edmod wodstok wyst thynge syr edwarde broder deed whervpon toke lettre kyng edward broder worthy lorde receyued lettre hy behight hym message wtout ony fayle syr edmond toke leue foresayd iohn went cou tre lordshyp kent anone iohn wyst syr edmond gone kent lordship went haste might fro castel corf came syr roger mortimer toke hym lettre syr edmond wodstok erle kent taken hym closed ensealed wt owne seale whan syr roger mortimer receyued lettre vnclosed sawe conteyned therin began rede wherof begynynge p worshyps reuerence broders legeaunce subie cyon syr knyght worshipful dere broder yf please praye hertely ye good com forte shall ordeyne ye shall come prison deliuered disease ye vnderstande grete lordshyp haue myne assentyng almoost grete lordes englonde theyr apparayle saye armure wt tresour without nombre maynteyne quarell ferforth ye shall kynge agayn ye haue sworne vpo boke well prelate erles baron whan syr roger mortimer sawe vnderstode myght strengthe lettre anone herte wrath began boll euyll hert bare toward syr edmond wodstok erle kent wt haste might went vnto dame isabell quene kynges moder shewed syr edmondes lettre wyll purpose coniected ordeyned put downe kyng edward wyndsore sone ryalte kyngdom certes syr roger sayd hath syr edmod done faders soule sayd wyll therof auenged yf god graut lyfe shorte tyme quene isabel went king edward sone parlyament wynchestre amende wronges trespaces done amonge people realme toke shewed hym lettre syr edmond wodstock made ensealed owne seale badde hym vpon blessynge sholde auenged vpon syr edmonde vpon deedly enemy quene sore wroth towarde syr edmonde erle kent cessed neuer praye vnto sone tyll sent haste hym vpon kyng sent lettres syr edmond wodstok sholde come speke wt hym wynchestre maner thynges lefte whan syr edmond sawe king sent hym lettres ensealed hasted hym myght tyll came wynchestre whan quene wyst syr edmonde comen wynchestre anone went prayed fast vnto kynge edwarde sone good erle arested anone ladde vnto barre robert hamond crowner kynges housholde assocyed hym syr roger mortimer spake fore sayd robert said syr edmond erle kent ye shall vnderstade done v wyte prycypally vnto lyege lorde kynge edwarde englonde almyghty god hym saue kepe ye deedly enemy traytour also comyn enemy vnto realme ye haue ben aboute many daye make preuy delyuerauce syr edward somtyme king englonde broder whiche somtyme put downe royalte comyn assent lordes englonde appeasynge lorde kynges estate also realme answered good man sayd forsothe syr vnderstande well neuer traytour kyng ne realme god worlde therfore kynges leue shall preue defende man ought sayd mortymer syr edmonde ferforth knowen may well gaynsayd presence shall well proued fals mortimer lettre syr edmond taken syr iohn daueryll castell corf take kyng edward broder syr edmonde wyst ne supposed nothynge syr iohn daueryll ben fals deliuer lettre suche wyse mortimer thought maner thynge lettre mortimer sayd syr edmonde shewed lettre sealed asked yf knewe lettre seale syr edmod loked theron auysed hym longe tyme print seale myght se lettre wtin wyst well seale thought lettre borne grete charge thought nothynge lettre sayd openly herynge ye forsothe seale wyll forsake loo sayd mortymer syrs ye hath sayd knowlegeth lettre seale ye shall conteyned therin mortimer opened lettre folden fore togyder red openly worde worde hering whan lettre red sayd loo syrs ye haue herde wryten hath knowleged lettre seale may go therfro cryed gaue dome sholde hanged drawen heed smytte maner traytour heyres dysheryted euermore ladde forth put pryson whan done quene wyst dampned waye lawe bothe lyf lymme heyres dysheryted euer open knowlegynge playn court wherfore thought good foresayd syr edmond hastely slayne without wytynge kyng el kynge wolde lyghtly forgyue hym deth sholde turne moche sorowe empeched anone quene counseyle mortimer wtout ony counseyle sente haste baylyfe wynchestre sholde sinyte syr edmondes heed wod ok erle kent without ony maner abydynge respyte vpon payne lyfe lymme shold haue none execucyon bycause taryenge withstandyng iudgement toke baylyfe syr edmond pryson ladde hym besyde castel wynchestre made gongfermer smyte dyed none durst dyed ala whyle say day october thyrde yere kyng edwardes regne whan kyng wyst therof wonder sory let bury hym ye frere minours winchestre p deth syr roger mortymer erle marche befell tyme syr roger mortimer erle marche proude hawteyne helde lord realme pere became couetous folowed dame isabell quenes courte kyng edwardes moder beset penyworthes wt offycers quenes houshold maner kynges officer dyd made takyng touchynge vytayles also caryages dyd bycause e pen gadre tresour dyd without nombre myght made hym wonder preuy quene isabell moche lordshyp retynue grete lordes englonde hym adrad wherfore kynge couseyle towardes hym agreued ordeyned amonge vndo hym pure reason lawe bycause kynge edward kynges fader tray oursly hym murdred castell corf sayd playnly parte boke deth kynges counseyle loued mortimer tolde hym preuite kyng counseyle aboute fro daye daye hym destroye vndo wherfore mortimer sore anoyed angry deuyll agaynst yt ye kynges couseyle sayd wolde auenged euer toke longe afterward king edward dame philip wyfe dame isabell kynges moder syr roger mortymer ne went vnto notyngham soiourne befel quene isabell counseyle mortimer toke key ye gate ye castel notyngham man myght come nyght comaudement mortimer ne ye kynge none couseyle tyme befell mortimer deuyll wrath boyled also wrath ye agaynst kynges men pryncypally agaynst yt accused hym kyng ye deth syr edward fader pryuely counseyle taken bytwene quene isabell mortymer bysshop lyncolne syr symond bedford syr hugh trompyngton preuy theyr couseyle vndo al ye accused mortimer vnto ye kynge faders deth treason felony wherfore yt kynges couseyle wha wyst mortimer castynge pryuely came kyng edwarde sayd mortimer wolde destroye bycause accused hym kyng edwardes deth fader prayed hym yt wolde maynteyne theyr right lordes yt pursued quarell syr willia mountagu syr vmfrey de boghun syr willia broder syr rauf stafford syr robert herford syr willyam clynton syr iohn neuyll nornby many theyr consent swore vpon boke maynteyne quarell moche myght befell syr wyllyam mountagu ne none ye kynges frendes must herborowed castel mortimer went toke theyr herborowe dyuers place ye towne notyngham tho sore adrad lest mortimer shold destroye haste came vnto kyng edward syr willyam moutagu yt ye castell pryuely tolde hym none company sholde take mortimer without counseyle helpe wyllyam eland constable castell truly sayd ye king loue well therfore counseyle ye go foresayd constable comaunde hym name frende helpe take mortimer thynge left vpon peryll lyfe lymme sayd moutagu syr lord graut mercy went forth foresayd moutagu came constable castell told hym kynges wyll answered sayd kynges wyll shold done moche myght wolde spare maner deth swore made othe sayd syr willyam mountagu constable herynge helpyng vnto quarell certes dere frende v behoueth werke aduyse take mortymer syth ye keper castell haue key warde syr sayd constable ye shall vnderstande ye gate castell ben locked locke dame isabell sente hyther nyght hath key therof layeth vnder leuesell bedde tyll morowe ye may come castell gate maner wyse knowe aley stretcheth warde vnder ye erth ye foresayd castel yt goth ye west whiche aley dame isabell quene ne none men mortymer ne none copany knoweth shall lede ye aley ye shall come castel wtout espyenge ony men yt enemyes nyght syr william moutagu lordes quarell constable also wente hors made semblaut go mortimer syght anone mortimer herde tydynges wende yt wold haue gone ouer see fere hym anone company toke cou seyle amonge lette theyr passage sent lettres anone porte none grete lordes sholde go home theyr coutrees yf arested taken amoge thynges willyam eland constable ye foresayd castell priuely lad syr william moutagu company foresayd waye vnder erth tyl came castel went vp toure mortymer syr hugh trompyngton theym escryed hydously sayd traytours nought ye come castell ye shall dye yet euyl deth euerychone anone one yt mountagues copany mace smote hugh vpon ye heed yt brayn brast fell ye groude dyed euyll dethe toke mortymer armed hym ye toures dore whan herde ye noyse drede whan quene isabell sawe ye mortymer taken made moche sotowe hert wordes sayd fayr syrs pray yt ye harme body worthy knyght welbeloued frende dere cosyn tha went then came brought mortimer presented hym vnto kynge edward comaunded brynge hym safe warde anone consentyng vnto mortimer doynge herde tell yt taken went hydde p urly nyght wente towne eueryche countree heuy herte mournyng chere lyued vpon theyr londes well myght yere yt mortymer taken retynue ix score knyghtes without squyers sergeauntes armes fote men mortymer ladde london syr symond bedford ladde hym taken constable toure kepe afterwarde mortymers lyf examyned westmynster kynge grete lordes englonde peryll myght fall realme enquyre also whiche consentynge syr edwardes deth kynges fader also whome scottes escaped fro scanhope scotlonde without wyll kyng edward also yt charter ragman delyuered vnto scottes wherin homage frautees ye lordes scotlonde conteyned scottes sholde euer vnto englysshe kynge realme scotlode wherfore absence dampned draw hanged treason myschefe came hym saynt andrewes euen yere ye incarnacyon lorde iesu chryst ccc rxx p kyng edward gate agayn vnto hym gracyously ye homage f au e scotlonde wherof put false couseyle quene isabell moder syr roger mortymer newly made erle march haue ye herd syr iohn bayloll tyme pea chosen kyng scotlonde bycause came ye eldest doughter erle dauid huntyngton yt kyng alysaunders broder scotlond yt dyed without heyre body begoten iohn made feaute homage kyng edward henryes sone ye thyrde londes scotlonde afterwarde wtsayd homage couseyle scottes yere lorde cc lxxiiij sent vnto pope fals suggestion made othe vnto foresayd kyng edward ouer estate wyl whiche othe ye pope hym assoyled bulles hy sent anone kyng edward wyst therof ordeyned anone baron came barwyk conquered towne whiche conquest slayne xxv vij c bayloll yt kyng scotlonde came yelded hym good kynge edward kyng afterward delyuered ye toure london ye grete lordes wt hym tho taken barwyk gaue saufconduyte go scotlonde scottes ith theyr falsnes warred vpon good kyng edward whan syr iohn bayloll kyng scotlonde sawe went ouer see vnto dunpier lyued vpon londes wel myght tyll yt scottes wold amede theyr mysoedes trespace ad wt hy syr edward sone wherfore ye scottes despyte hym called hym syr iohn turnlabaerd bycause wolde offende ne trespace agaynst ye good kyng edward englonde forsoke realme scotlonde set therof lytel pryce syr iohan dwelled longe tyme frauce tyll yt dyed syr edward sone receyued herytage dyd homage ye kyng frauce londes dunpier befell afterward edward yt iohn baylols sone wt hym squyer englode borne yorkshyre yt called iohn barnaby edwarde bayloll loued hym moche nygh hym full preuy iohn barnaby debate frensshe man ye towne dupier slewe hym went waye ye haste yt myght ye castell haue helpe lord anone came ye officer ye towne take iohn barnaby felon syr edward lord holpe hym rescowed hym night made go ye castell went waye came englonde wtout ony harme whan ye kyng frauce sawe yt syr edward rescowed felon became wonder wrothe agaynst syr edward anone let arest hym toke hades londes dwelled syr edward pryson vnto ye tyme yt syr henry beaumont came frauce whiche henry somtyme erle angos scotlonde wyfe put therof wha ye accordemet bytwene englonde scotlond quene isabell roger mortimer theyr copany ye maryage yt made bytwene dauyd yt robert ye brus sone dame ione ye toure kyng edwardes syster englode well vnderstode yt ye ende shold come ryght yf syr edwarde bayloll yt ryght heyre ye realme scotlonde kyng fraunce lowys loued moche syr henry hym ful preuy thought make delyuerauce syr edwarde bayloll yf myght ony maner wyse tho prayed ye kyng ye wolde please noble grace graut hym syr edward baylols body vnto ye next parlyament myght lyue wt tentes meane tyme yt myght stande iudged wt peres ye parlyament ye kyng grauted hym prayer made foresayd edward delyuered pryson maner aboue said anone prison syr henry toke hym forth wt hym ladde hym englode made hym dwell pryuely ye maner sandhall vpon ouse yorkeshyre lady vescy ordeyned huge retynue englysshemen also alyens conquere agayne herytage gaue moche siluer sowdyours alyens helpe hym behyght helpe hym yt myght fayled hym moost nede yt tyme donald erle moryf herde tell yt syr edwarde baylol priuely come englode came hym made grete ioye comynge agayn sayd hym behyght hym yt ye grete lordes scotlonde shold hym attendaut shold holde hym kynge ryght heyre scotlode dyd hy homage feaute came syr henry beaumont kynge edwarde englonde prayed hym ye waye charite wolde graut grace syr edward bayloll myght safely go londe fro sandhal vnto scotlode coquere ryght herytaunce scotlonde kynge answered sayd yf suffre bayloll go londe scotlonde people wold saye yt shold assentyng vnto ye company syr praye ye wolde gyue hym leue take wt hym sowdyours englysshe yt myght safely lede hy londe scotlode syr vpon couenaunt yt yf befall god forbydde dyscomfyted batayle scottes also ye lordes holde wt bayloll ben euer rente haue englonde ye kyng vpon couenaunt graunted theyr bone touchynge hym yt quarell whiche claymed haue londes rente ye realme scotlode ye name lordes pursued foresayd quarell yt saye syr edward bayloll whiche chalenged realme scotlonde syr henry beaumot erle angos syr dauid stroboly erle atheles syr frey mombray walter comyn many yt put rytage scotlonde whan ye made bytwene englonde sayd ye shall lordes toke wt v c armes ij archer tho wente shyppe sayled see tyll vnto scotlonde came londe kehorne xij myle sayn ioh towne anone sente theyr pe agayne sholde hurt ne empayred neyther man sholde go ye shyppes agayn though nede abyde ee stande rather deth tha flee mayn quarell whan erle fi man sterne herde comen take londe scotlonde came haste kynkehorne xij scottes destroye hym sholde come londe syr edwarde bayloll company dyscomfyted hym ye whiche discomfyture syr alysauder seron slayne many erle fyffe tho sore full yll ashamed lytell company dyscomfy hym shamefully put hym company alyue flee came syr edward bayloll toke ye coun tre aboute hym tyll came vnto abbey dunfermelin foude vytayles hym folke amonge thyges foude chambre aboute v c grete staues fyne oke longe pykes yren stele toke deliuered moost strongest men copany anone went then lodged hym felde two myle fro saynt iohannes towne whan burgeyses towne herde erle fiffe dyscofyted bayloll fore adrad brake theyr brydges yt made ouer ye water erne baylol myght go ouer wherfore lodged hym yt nyght lytell hede toke rest sayd vnto people dere lordes ye knowe full well lodged bytwene enemyes yf may v hampre bote deth wherfore yf abyde styll nyght wene shall turne v moche harme ye power scotlonde may euer wexe encreace may lytell people agaynst wherfore praye ye loue almighty god make v bolde hardy yt may myghtely take scottes night boldly warre vpon let v pursue nyght yf v trauayled se hardynes scottes se trauayled wery sorer wyll adrad wt v fyght fyersly shall fyght pursue yt grace god al worlde shall speke dough tyne chyuairy syrs vnderstande well al company came syr edward bayloll grauted well couseyle therof ryght glad anone pursued vpon scottes became wonder wery bayloll company sore folowed moche harme sorow theyr assaut myght feblenes helpe lytell people tho sayd scottes amonge befall lytell people bayloll hathe wynge dothe v moche trauayle sorowe certes semeth v werketh grace wonder gracyous quarell certes shal deed may come hy v yelde syth fader set v pryce amonge thynges bayloll people passed water erne syr roger swynerton sone fyers angry went forth sawe people armes full well arayed forth went vnto faught slewe toke many wolde abyde neuertheles yt assaut wende ben grete hoost scotlonde whan came morowe gadred togyder rested whyle whyle ye englisshmen rested noble baron thomas vescy noble baron stafford pricked theyr horse vp ye hylles kepe estres coutree prycked vp sawe grete hoost good araye ordeyned theyr wynges helmes sheldes shynynge comynge vpon came tho two lordes agayn baylols folke sayd loue god good coforte ye shall haue batayle anone right tho spake syr fouke ye sone gareyne baron grete renome dedes armes syrs vnderstade wyll saye haue seen many dyuers wynges wel amonge sarasyns iewes amonge scottes yet sawe neuer fourth parte wynge fyght therfore yf ye wyll abyde enemyes ynough fight yf good hert good courage lost therfore loue god let v take v good herte let v bolde thynke neuer wyues ne childre onely coquere enemyes batayle helpe lorde god shall ouercome yt came hoost scottes towarde full surely agaynst syr edward bayloll thre bataylles well arayed armure wonder fyersly came towarde baylols company wha syr donald erle marcil scottes sawe said robert brus sone robert brus wordes syr roberte sayd full sore forthynketh herte yt people bayloll hathe brought wt hym sholde dye dynt scottes swerdes lyth yt chrysten men therfore thyketh yt grete charite sende vnto yelde mercy raunsom greuous raunsom moche haue take londe done yll certes sayd syr robert brus haue wel perceyued yu art enemy traytour scotlonde syth yu wylt consent saue deedly enemyes yt haue done v moche sorowe shame semeth well ye theyr assent certes roberte sayd syr donald falsly ye lye theyr company ne theyr cosent hastely ye shall se wyll fyght wt rather ony copany certes syr roberte sayd shal maugre thy heed assayle thou prycked theyr stedes fyersly gaskmo theyr wynges folowed rege tho came mette wt bayloll copany hangynge bough strayte passage fast hasted vnto englysshmen thousandes fell groude eche ouer hepe bothe hors syr bayloll men myghtely stode agaynst fast slewe scottes groude many fore wouded longe tyll stode vpon foyned wt theyr swerdes speres theyr bodyes full sore trauayled vpon tyll yt became woders wery wyst scottes lefte alyue fledde away saue themselfe best maner myght tho pursued syr edwarde ba men slewe tyll night fro then went saynt iohns towne toke helde vytayled themselfe theyr owne wyll foude ynough wher make mery made bayloll men yt wounded go shyppe sayle englonde theyr woudes tyme flemyng see stronge thefe robber yt called crab flem dryue flaudres wyckednes therfore came scotlond holde scottes dyd e harme englisshme myght crab mette bay e men see yt wouded baray e sent agayn englonde hele theyr woudes crab gaue grete assaure wold haue slayne englysshmen defended manfully dyscofyced crab copany fledde scotlonde came towarde saynt iohns towne foude grete copany scottes yt comen agayn togyder discomfyture gaskemore whiche besyeged bayloll men towne saynt iohn anone tolde scottes discofyted englysshmen wou ded gaskmore went towarde englonde hele theyr woudes sayd scottes yt sholde haue power ne myght grace agaynst edwarde bayloll bycause dyscomfyted empayred chiualry scotlonde handfull men accompte agaynst scottes slayne wherfore couseyled remeue siege saynt iohns towne kepe best maner myght scottes vnderstode yt crab sayd sothe forsoke ye syege went then nyght holpe themselfe best maner yt myght whan thyge knowen scotlonde lordes knyghtes discofyted gaskmore scotlond syr edward bayloll ye shall vnderstande ye lordes ladyes gentyls scotlonde came wonder fast saynt iohns towne yelded bayloll dyd homage feaute theyr londes yelded pea receiued frely fro then went ye abbey scone crowned kyng scotlonde let crye pea throughout londe yt tyme befell kynge edward helde parlyament amonge lyeges newe castell vpon tyne amende trespaces wronges yt ben done londe syr edward bayloll king scotlonde came hym thyder dyd hym homage feaute realme scotlonde maner kyng edward englode gadred agayn homage feautees scotlond wherof put counseyle assent dame isabell moder syr roger mortimer erle marche toke baylol kyng scotlonde leue kynge edward englonde went then owne londe scotlonde set lytell suche couseyled holpen hym quarell wherfore went hym went lyued theyr londes rente scotlond befell longe afterward king scotlonde ne remeued came toure anand toke dwellyng thyder came hym copany knyghtes stronge men worthy yelded vnto kyng bare fayre dede coutenauce trusted moche vpon anone ye traytours sawe yt trusted moche vpo ordeyned amoge fyfty company wolde haue slayne theyr lord kyng grace almighty god brake wall hole chambre god wolde escaped theyr trechery men slayne escaped wt moche drede vnto ye towne cardoyll helde hy sore anoyed befell ladyes euen ye concepcyon sent kyng edward bayloll kyng edward englode falsly traytoursly lytell tyme put shame sorow lyege men trusted wonder moche prayed hy loue god yt wolde maynteyn hym helpe hym agaynst enemyes kyng englode hym grete pyte behyght helpe socour hym sent hym worde shold holde hym foresayd cite cardoyll tyll gadred power ordeyned kynge edwarde englonde counseyle london let gadre men dyuers shyres englonde whan redy went toward towne barwyk vpon twede thyder came vnto hym kynge edward bayloll scotlonde power besyeged towne made without towne fayre towne pauylyons dy ched drede scottes made many assautes wt gonne engynes towne wherwt destroyed many fayre house chirches also beten downe erth grete stone spytefully came gonne engynes neuertheles scottes kept well towne ye two kynges myght come therin longe tyme kynges abode loge tyll wtin town fayled vitayles also wery wakynge yt wyst ye shall vnderstand yt scottes yt towne barwyk comyn cou seyle theyr assent let crye vpon walles towne yt myght haue pea englysshmen therof prayed kyng grace mercy prayed hy trewse viij dayes vpon couenaut yt yf rescowed yt syde towne toward scotlonde scottes within viij dayes yt wold yelde vnto ye kyng towne also hold couenaut profred king xij hostage towne barwyk whan hostage delyuered kyng anone towne sent scottes told theyr sorowe myschefe scottes came priuely ouer water twede bought abbey syr willyam diket yt tho steward scotlonde many yt came wt hym put themselfe grete peryll theyr lyues yt tyme came ouer brydge yt broken stone away many theyr company drowned foresayd wyllyam went ouer copany came shippes englonde slewe barge hull xvj men went towne barwik ye water syde wherfore scottes helde towne rescowed asked theyr hostage agayn kyng englonde kynge sente worde agayne asked theyr hostage wt wronge syth came towne englode syde couenaut bytwene yt towne shold rescowed ye halfe scotlonde anone comauded kyng edward yelde towne wold hange hostage scottes sayd towne rescowed well ynough therto wold holde whan kyng edward sawe scottes breke theyr couenaut made wonder wroth anone let take syr thomas fitz willyam syr alyfauder feton wardeyn barwyk whiche thomas parsone dunbar let taken fyrst afore hostage cause syr alysaunders faders keper towne tho comaunded euery daye two hostage towne tyll done dethe yf yelded towne sholde teche breke theyr couenaut wha towne herde tydynges became wonder sory sent kyng yt wolde graut v dayes respyte bytwene tho hondred men arntes xx armes myght strength go bytwene towne barwik force vitayle ye towne must holde restowed yf xxj xxij slayne tho c beforesayd ye towne sholde holden restowed couenaut holde sent hym xij foresayd towne hostage kyng grauted theyr prayer toke hauens went ouer see dyuers lode eche waye ye duke norfolke went venise died whose soule god haue mercy amen kynge rychard made clerke syr roger walden arche bysshop cauterbury p xxij yere kynge richardes regne fals couseyle ymaginacyon couetous men aboute hym made ordeyned blancke chartres made ensealed al maner ry men throughout ye realme moche yt compelled diuers people set theyr seales therto done grete couetyse wherfore al good hertes ye realme clene turned away fro ye kyng euer vtter destruccyon ende hym yt hygh excellent prynce kyng couetous fals couseyle falsely betrayed ala pyte ye suche kynge myght se kynge rychard set kyngdome ryall londe englonde ferme vnto foure persones whiche syr wyllya scrope erle wylshyre tresourer englond syr iohn busshe henry grene syr iohn bagot knyghtes whiche turned myschefe deth within lytell tyme ye shall fynde afterwarde wryten p kyng rychard de grete ordynauce went hymself ouer see irlonde many grete lordes wt hym grete hoostes strength theyr kynge wt men armes archer moche grete stuffe ryght good ordynauce longed vnto warre passed ouer ye see ordeyned made edmond langley vncle ye duke yorke lewtenau englonde absence gouernauce cousey e iiij knyghtes yt taken englonde ferme kyng passed see came irlonde well worth ly receyued rebelles ben called irysshmen came downe kynge yelded bothe body go de owne wyll swore vnto lyege men dyd hym homage feaute good seruyce thus coquered ye moost parte irlende lytell tyme whyle kyng chard thus irlonde syr henry bolyngbroke erle derby ye kyng made duke herford che duke kyng exiled londe comen agayn englonde chalenge ye dukedom lancast right true herytage came downe frauce vnto alays mette hy syr thomas arundell yt archebysshop exiled englond wi hym came erle arundel heyre whiche kepynge syr iohn shelley knight somtyme wt erle huntyngdon wt duke excestre whiche tho castell gate sussex stale awaye came calays well worthely kepte tyll two lordes come calays tha worthy duke archebysshop cau terbury arundell shypped ye hauen calais drewe theyr course northward arryued yorkshyre rauensporne fast wydelyngton came entred fyrst londe two lordes hym theyr meyny moche people realme herde comynge knewe yt anone drewe vnto hym welcomed lordes couraged maner thynge passed forth londe gadred moche people whan kyng rychard herde wyst two lordes comen agayne englonde londed kynge lefte ordynauce irlonde came englondward haste myght came castell lyut abode take counseyle myght done hym came none wha syr thomas percy erle worcestre yt ye kynges steward wyst knewe anone came hall amonge ye people brake yerde ye ryall kynges housholde anone euery man disperpied went waye forsoke theyr mayster souerayn lorde lefte hym alone thus kynge rycharde brought downe destroyed stode hym selfe alone without comforte socour ony good counseyle ony man ala pite ryall kyng anone came tydyges syr henry boling broke vp stronge power people ye squyers englonde reysed vp shyres strengthyng hym agaynst kyng rychard thus soone comen north coutree brystowe mette syr wyllyam scrope erle wylshyre tresourer englonde syr iohn busshe syr henry grene iohn bagot escaped fro went ouer see irlonde thre knyghtes taken theyr herdes smytten thus died theyr fals couetyse kynge rychard taken brought vnto duke anone ye duke put hy fast warde stronge holde vnto comynge london westmynster ryall chare couered blacke veluet baners dyuers armes horse drawing chare trapped blacke beten dyuers armes many torche brennynge waye tyll came westmynster let make hym ryall solempne enterement buryed hym quene anne wyfe owne desyre ferther syde saynt edwardes yne abbey saynt peter westmynster vpon whose soule god haue mercy p yere certayne lollers taken fals heretykes yt purposed false treason haue slayne kyng haue destroyed clergy realme myght haue theyr false purpose lorde god wolde suffre haste kynge warnynge therof theyr fals ordinauce werkyng came sodeynly power sayt iohns without sinythfelde anone toke certayn lollers fals heretykes brought ye kynges presence tolde theyr fals purpose ordynauce wolde haue done wrought yf myght haue regned theyr wyl told whiche theyr capytayns gouernours ye king comauded toure londo toke moo bothe win ye cite wtout sent newgate bothe co ters brought examinacion afore ye clergy kynges iustyces couicte theyr fals heresy dampned iustyee theyr fals treason theyr iudgemet yt sholde drawen fro ye toure london saint giles felde hanged brent ye galowes also taken syr roger acton knyght heresy eke treason agaynst ye kyng ye realme came afore clergy couict heresy brent dampned iustyces drawen toure london cite saynt giles felde hanged brent p ye seconde yere kynge henryes regne held couseyle ye lordes ye realme westmyster put hym demaude prayed besouhgt theyr goodnes theyr good couseyle good wyll shewe hym touchyng ye tytell right yt normandy gascoyn guyen whiche ye king frauce whelde wrongfully vnryghtfully whiche auncestres hy true tytell coquest right herytage whiche normady gascoyn guyen ye good kyng edward wyndsore auncestres hym holden theyr lyf tyme lordes gaue hym couseyle sende embassadours kyng frauce couseyle yt shold gyue vp vnto hym ryght herytage yt saye normandy gascoyn guyen whiche predecessours holden afore hy el wold wynne strengthe swerde shorte tyme ye helpe almighty god dolphyn frauce answered embassadours saydi maner kyng ouer yonge tender age make ony warre agaynst hy lyke yet good warryour make suche coquest vpon hym somwhat scorne despyte sent hy tonne full tenes balles bycause shold haue somwhat playe withall lordes wolde become hym better mayntayn ony warre anone lordes yt embassadours toke theyr leue came englonde agayne tolde kynge couseyle vngoodly answere yt dolphin present whiche sente kynge whan kynge herde theyr wordes answere dolphyn wonder sore agreued ryght euyll apayed towarde frensshmen towarde kynge dolphyn thought auege hym soone god wold sende hym grace myght anone let make tenes balles dolphyn haste myght grete gonstones dolphyn playe withall anone kynge sent lordes helde grete couseyle westmynster told answer yt dolphin worthy present yt sent hym lordes playe wtall ye kyng lordes accorded shold redy armes wt theyr power best araye yt myght done gete men armes archer myght goten stuffe yt longed warre redy wt theyr retynue mete southhampton lamasse nexte folowynge without ony delaye wherfore ye kynge ordeyned nauy shyppes maner stuffe vytayle loged suche warryour maner ordynaunce hauen southhampton ye nombre ccc xx sayles tha fell grete dysease foule myschefe thre lordes whiche kyng trusted moche false couetyse purposed ymagined kynges deth thought haue slayne hym bretherne taken see whiche thre lordes named thus syr rycharde erle cambrydge broder ye duke yorke ye seconde lord scrope tresourer englode thyrd sir thomas gray knyght north coutree thre lordes aforesayd lucre money made promesse vnto frensshmen haue slayne kyng henry fyfth bretherne false trayne sodeynly ben ware almyghty god grete grace helde holy hande ouer saued perillous meiny haue done receyued frensshmen millyon gold openly proued theyr fals treason thre iudged deth iudgement sholde ladde hampton without northgate heded thus ended theyr lyues theyr fals couetyse treason anone done kynge meyny made redy went shyppe sayled forth xv hondred shyppes arryued within seyne kydecause vpon ladyes euen assumpcyon normandy wt ordynauce went forth harflet besyeged towne londe also water sent capytayne towne charged hym delyuer towne ye capytayne sayd delyuered hym none ne none wolde hy yelde badde hym best kyng layde ordinauce vnto towne saye gonne engynes tripgettes shotte cast walles eke towne cast downe bothe toures towne layde erth played tenes hard gonne stone towne whan sholde playe theyr songe well away ala euer ony suche tenes balles made cursed al tho warre began tyme euer borne p morowe kyng let crye euery gate towne euery man shold redy morowe erly make assaute towne willyam boucher iohn graut xij worthy burgeses came kyng besought hym ryall pryncehode power withdrawe malyce bestruccyon dyd besought hym viij dayes respyte trewse yf ony rescowe myght come el yelde vp ye towne hym wt al theyr goodes kyng sent forth capytayne kepte remenaut styll wt hym lord gaucorte yt capytayne towne went forth roen ye haste vnto dolphyn helpe socour none ne man rescowe dolphyn wold abyde thus capytayne came agayne vnto kynge yelded vp ye towne delyuered hym key called vncle ye erle dorset made hym capytayne town harflet deliuered key bad hy go put fresshe people bothe men wome child stuffe town harflet wt englysshe people ye kyng sent englode let crye euery good town englode crafty wold come thyder enhabyte hym town shold haue houshold hy heyres euer thyder went many marchautes crafty enhabyted strength towne welcome wha kyng sawe town well stuffed bothe vytayles men worthy prince toke leue went toward calays lond frensshmen herde comynge thought haue stopped hy waye sholde passe waye haste myght brake al bridge ony passage hors man moche myght man passe ouer ryuers neyther hors ne fo e yf shold haue bendrowned therfore king wt people went sought way ferre vp toward paris ryall power frauce assembled redy gyue hym batayle destroye people almyghty god guyde saued hy meyny defended hym enemyes power purpose thanked god saued owne knyght kyng ryght full tytel kyng beholdyng seynge grete multytude nombre enemyes withstande waye gyue hym batayle kyng wt meke herte good spiryte lyfte vp handes almyghty god besought hy helpe daye saue true seruautes kynge gadred lordes people aboute bad al good chere shold haue fayre gracyous victory better theyr enemyes prayed make redy batayle wolde rather dye daye felde taken enemyes wold neuer put realme englonde rausom persone duke yorke fell knee besought kyng bone wold graut hym yt daye vautward batayle kyng grauted hym askyng sayd gramercy cosyn yorke prayed hym make hym redy badde euery man ordeyn hym stake tree sharpe bothe endes stake myght pyght erth slope theyr enemyes shold ouer come horsback yt theyr fals purpose arayed ouer ryde meyny sodeynly fyrst comyng first brunt al nyght batayle frensshmen made many grete fyers moche reuell howting showting played kyng lordes dyse archer alwaye blanke theyr money wend al theyrs morne ose daye gan sprynge kyng good aduyse let araye batayle wynges charged euery man kepe hole togyder prayed good chere wha redy asked tyme ye daye said pryme sayd kyng good tyme al englod prayeth v therfore good chere let v go iourney tha sayd wt hye voyce name almighty god saynt george auaut baner saynt george day thyne helpe frensshmen came pryckynge downe wold haue ouer rydden meyny god archer made ryght soone stomble archer shotte neuer arowe amysse perysshed brought ye groude bothe hors man shotte yt daye wager stake made toppe ouer terue eche one ouer ouer laye hepes two speres length heyght kyng wt meyny men armes archer yt thacked thycke arowes layde wt stake kyng handes fought manly daye thus almyghty god saynt george brought enemyes groude gaue v daye victory slayne frensshmen yt daye ye felde agincourt xi without prysoners yt take nombred daye frensshmen felde moo syxe score god daye fought v came tydynges kynge newe batayle frensshmen ordeyned redy stele hym came towardes hym anone kyng let crye euery man sholde slee prysouers taken anone araye batayle agayne redy fyght frensshmen whan frensshmen sawe men kylled downe theyr prysoners withdrewe brake theyr batayle al theyr araye thus kyng worthy conquerour daye victory elde agincourt pycardy kynge returned agayn batayle e people slayne englysshmen yf ony hurte myght holpen deed felde duke barry duke alauson duke braband erle nauerne thefe constable frauce viij erles archebysshop saunce good baron c mo worthy knyghtes grete alyaunce cote armures xv hodred englysshmen deed yt daye good duke yorke erle suffolke englysshmen deed passyng xxvi bodyes thanked god batayle frydaye whiche saynt crispyne crispinians day moneth october anone kynge comauded bury duke yorke caryed forth wt hym erle suffolke prysoners duke orlyauce duke burbon erle vendome erle ewe erle richemond syr sigaut marsha f frauce many worthy lordes taken batayle agincourt brought towne calays ouer see wt kyng englonde londed douer kent wt prysoners eth well worthely arayed welcome kyng dyuers melodyes hanked almyghty god gracyous vyctory shewed hym kyng prisoner passed forth ty came saynt thomas wateryng mette wt hym religyous men wt processyon welcomed hym kyng came rydyng prysoners rite londo shewed many fayre syght yt condythes yt crosse chepe heuenly araye augels archaugels patriarkes prophetes virgyns wt diuers melodyes sensyng syngynge westmynster mayre toke leue kyng rode home agayne p thyrde yere kyng heryes regne fyfth came emperour almayn kyng rome hungry englonde e london mayre alderman wt sheryues worthy craftes london kynges vpon paules steple london yere moneth august ye kynge wexed seke boy de vincene wha sawe sholde dye made testamet ordeyned many noble thinges soule deuoutly receyued al cheryghtes holy chirche ferforth whan anoynted sayd seruyce preest verse psalme iserere mei deus benigne fac dne bona volutate tua syon vt edificetur muri hierusalem badde tary sayd thus good lorde thou knowest myn entent ne v marchaut yt shold go flaudres go calais tha calais made mayster denham many go sandwyche dyd assayled towne water londe gate brought capytayn ouer see smote heed yet dayly men came ouer fro londo armed let ye lordes ye kyges couseyle knowe theyr treuth also theyr entent assembled tolde yt enteded harme kynges sone saue yt wolde put hym suche sone aboute hym departed fro london grete paynes purgatory yf enioyned hym penauce shal neuer suffre paynes hell dye fynally wtout tepentauce synne ye ensample set ful ende chap te p treuisa truly man may saued yf repetaut someuer penaunce euery man repentaut lyues ende shal sekerly saued though neuer saynt patrykes purgatory ylonde connacte sa see conaccina halowed say brandon hath myce deed bodyes ben buryed kepte erth rotte mamoma welle wassheth hym wt waterof welle shall hoore heed well vltonia someuer wasshen therin shall neuer wexe hoore afterwarde welle moustre mamoma yf ny man touche well anone shall fall grete rayne prouynce rayne shall neuer cesse tyll preest ne mayden synge masse chapell fast blysse water mylke one yere besprynge welle reconcyle welle straunge maner glyndal aboute oratory saynt keywyn wytches bere apple apple tree ben holsome sauery holy sayne brought forth apple prayer childe seke lake vlster moche fysshe therin whiche xxx myle length xv brede ryuer ban renneth lake north occean men saye lake began maner men yt countree yt euyll lyuynge coeuntes cu brutis welle londe grete reuerence olde tyme alwaye couered yf lefte vncouered well wold ryse drowne londe happed woman went yt welle fetche water hyed fast childe wepte cradell lefte welle vncouered ye welle sprange fast drowned ye woman chylde made coutree lake fysshe ponde preue ye sothe grete argument whan ye weder clere fysshers yt water se grounde vnder water rounde toures hygh shapen steples chirches londe north syde irlonde cou tree ossyryens euery vij yere prayer holy abbot twayne wedded man woman must nedes exyled forshapen lykenes wolues abyde vij yere ende vij yere yf lyue come home agayne take agayn theyr owne shape shall twayne go forth theyr stede forshapen vij yere lake londe yf poole tree pyght stycked therin parte shafte poole yt erth shall turne yren parte abydeth water shall turne stone parte abydeth aboue shall tree owne kynde also lake turneth h sell asshe asshe hasel yf done therin also irlonde thre lepes samons lepe st roche longe speres lengthe leg pond ben seen colmans byrdes byrdes called certelles come homely hande yf men wroug harme go away come agayn water shall bytter stynke dyd wronge shall astert without wreche myschefe yf amendes p touchynge saynt patrykes purgatory ye shall vnderstande seconde saynt patryke abbot bysshop whyle preched irlonde laboured studyen turne thylke wycked men lyued beestes theyr euyl lyfe drede paynes h coferme good lyf sayd wold turne myght knowe som grete paynes also blysse spake saynt patryke prayed almyghty god therfore lord iesu chryst appered saynt patryke toke hym staffe ladde hy wylde place shewed hym rounde pyt derke within sayd yf man repentaut stable byleue went pyt walked therin daye nyght sholde se sorowes paynes euyl men ioye blysse good men chryst vanisshed patrikes syght saynt patryke arered buylded chirche put therin chanons reguler closed pyt aboute wall chirche yerde eest ende chirche fast shette stronge dore man sholde nycely go without leue bysshop pryour place many men went came agayne saynt patrykes tyme tolde paynes ioye seen meruayles sawe ben yet wryten bycause therof many men turned conuerted ryght byleue also many men went came neuer agayne kyng stephen tyme kyng englonde knyght hyght owayne went saynt patrykes purgatory came agayn dwelled euer duryng lyfe nedes abbey ludensis ordre cysteaux tolde many wonder seen patrykes purgatory place called patrykes purgatory chirche named reglis man enioyned go purgatory couseyled sholde come therin take vpon hym penauce yf man haue auoided saable wyl nedes go therin shall fyrst go bysshop shall sent lettres pryoue place bothe shall couseyle hym leue yf wyll nedes go therto shall prayer fastynge xv dayes xv dayes shall houseled ladde dore purgatory processyon letany yet shall couseyled leue yf stedfast wyll en e dore shall opened blyssed go goddes name holde forth waye dore shall fast shette tyll nexte daye whan tyme pryour shall come open dore yf man comen ledeth hym chirche cessyon shall xv dayes prayer fastynge p meruayles sayntes irlonde ca xxix girald maketh mynde men nacyon ben angry men hasty take wreche whyles ben alyue sayntes halowes londe ben wrechefull sayntes londes clerkes londe ben chaste saye many prayer done grete abstynence daye drynke al nyght accouted myracle ery th wyne regneth ben chasen abbey clergy done monkes sholde ben yll ben worste good men amonge though ben fewe ben good ye best prelate countree ben full owe cor trespace besy cotemplacyon prechyng goddes worde therfore sayntes londe ben cofessours martyr amonge wonder al prelate londe clerkes prelate sholde vnknowen therfore wha put agaynst bysshop cassyll myght many sayntes ben irlonde neuer martyr amoge sythen men shrewed angry prelate recheles slowe cor eccyon trespace bysshop answered frowardly ynough sayd men ben shrewed angry ynough themselfe goddes seruautes ley neuer hade grete reuerence worshyp englyssh men come londe make martyr wont vse crafte p bisshop sayd bycause kyng henry seconde tho newe comen irlonde fresshely marty dome saynt thomas cauterbury p gir londe wale londe ben belle staues croked hedes suche thyges retykes grete reuerence worship men londe drede swere vpon one belle golden staues vpon gospel chefe suche relykes holden iesus staffe deuelyn whiche staffe say fyrst saynt patryke droue wormes irlond p aug de ci dei ca vij yf men e may dyuers maner beestes dyuers kynde kyndly goten bytwene male female come ben ylondes no flode men suppose suche beestes wame ylondes fyrst nexte forth el men saylynge ylondes brought suche beestes loue huntynge aungels god almyghtyes camaunde met brought suche beestes ylondes aboute erth brought forth fyrst fulfylled tho goddes comaundement comauded erth brynge forth grasse quycke beestes p endeth descripcyon brytayne whiche conteyneth englonde wale scotlond also bycause irloude vnder ule englonde olde tyme ath contynued ther fore haue set descripcyon sayd brytayn whiche haue taken cronycon bycause necessary vnto englysshemen knowe propertees modytees meruayles illya caxton haue set fyrst imprynt accordynge translacyon treuisa whiche request lorde
